Don Quixote mentions recognizing the family name from Fixer magazines, implying that at least one of Linton's siblings may be involved in some form of Fixer business.

---

## Lion

### Appearance
Lion is a tall woman with parted, spiky, blonde hair. She has a large scar on the left side of her chin. Under a long fur-lined coat, notably more ragged than her partner's coats, she wears a black turtleneck with two large purple belts made of snakeskin crossing over one another, golden buckles on each. She wears silver armor on her limbs, her gauntlets having long claws which she uses in combat.

### Personality
Lion is a confident, strong, person who has a tendency to become too emotional on jobs. She is excited to hunt people of a high caliber and wants to enjoy the thrill of killing such rare targets as much as possible.

### Story
Lion, Wolf, and Panther are met just as they corner Dante in a dark forest as a part of a plan made by their master. They decided to kill them once they realize that, thanks to Dante's new head, they will be unable to get any information out of them. Lion wanted to draw it out, but the other two believed it is best to kill them now. Just as Wolf was about to kill Dante, they heard a noise, realizing that a bus was heading towards them. Lion boasted that whoever is in that bus will pay a price for turning down the wrong road just before Mephistopheles hit her head-on. The Sinners exited the bus and engage the three in a fight, but Lion and her companions made short work of them and are only stopped when Vergilius dismembers Lion, taking an arm, and Wolf, removing her leg, before ordering Panther to drag them away in a retreat.

### Trivia
Panther, Lion and Wolf are based on the three beasts from the first Canto of Dante's Inferno, which symbolize the three major divisions of the sins punished in hell. The lion, the second beast encountered by Dante, represents violence, and is connected to the sins of pride and wrath.
Though their master is currently unknown, Vergilius referring to them as "the Serpent", as well as the presence of purple snake ornaments on all three group members, it is possible the identity of the master is none other than Iori, the Purple Tear.

---

## Lucio

### Appearance
Lucio is a tall man, with violet eyes and light gray hair split neatly to reveal his face, tied into a long ponytail that reaches his waist. He wears a Thumb uniform consisting of a rose-red vest, trousers, and a neatly buttoned ivory shirt fastened with a dark red tie, with his sleeves rolled up past his forearms. His hands are covered by rose-red gloves of the same color as his vest and trousers. His vest is fastened by two suspenders which connect to a belt, with a golden pin with one arrow pointing rightwards on his left breast. He carries two golden swords contained in wine-red scabbards, with gilded hilts and tips on the scabbards - one longsword with a striped pattern on his back, the other smaller with a spiral pattern at his left hip.

### Personality
Quiet and steadfast, Lucio carries an air of professionalism unlike his mentor. Even in the face of immense adversity and scolding, he remains calm and collected, ready to continue his efforts even while confronted by the possibility of loss. Given his role as a possible tutor, he is expected to be prim, proper, and dutiful. Though he frequently criticizes his opponents' forms in combat, his words are not as harsh as his master's, as he attempts to use them as a point of growth rather than disappointment.
Despite Valencina's abuse of Lucio, he feels permanently indebted to her for feeding and sheltering him, and is not willing to admit to her cruelness when asked. However, his combat passives demonstrate that he actually burns with resentment towards her, and has long been aware of her depravity, considering it his responsibility to eventually take her life.

### Story
**Prior to Limbus Company**

At one point in his life, Valencina rescued Lucio from the Backstreets, giving him food and a warm home while he was a nobody with little future.[1][2] This led Lucio to feel indebted to her and shaped his attitude toward his duties and her abuse. Despite this, he grew to silently resent his master, and repeatedly considered ending her life in her sleep. Lucio would eventually make up his mind to kill her after the House of Spiders completed their business with Limbus Company.[2]

**Canto IX: The Unsevering**

While Vergilius was out with Charon, Saude, and Pilot, Valencina and Lucio ambushed the group with the goal of keeping the Color Fixer occupied during the House of Spider's raid on the Limbus Company HQ. Knowing of Charon's importance to Vergilius, Valencina ordered her apprentice to kidnap and use her as a hostage. During this initial skirmish, Saude's arm was severed as she held on tightly to Charon, allowing Lucio to escape with the girl and then trail after Saude as she ran for backup.
Lucio was able to locate Saude within a truck typically used to transport members of the Before Team, which was then occupied by the Sinners. He destroyed the roof of the vehicle, falling into it with an unconscious Charon in his arms and with several Ring-provided manikins as battle help. Wasting no time, he engaged in battle with the Sinners, where he utilized the Palermitan Style in attempts to dispatch his enemies. Recognizing this style, Ryōshū questioned its use, before being informed of the man's status as her previous Nursefather's "textbook", aiming to replicate Ryōshū's abilities for her to re-learn the techniques. With this revelation, the Nursefather herself arrived on the scene and began scolding Lucio. As the two were not yet done fighting, Vergilius burst in shortly after, and began clashing with Valencina again.
Eventually, the Sinners were able to travel to Limbus Company HQ using the truck's Backdoor portal, and Lucio and Valencina stayed behind to continue distracting Vergilius. While Valencina related
her twisted views on Lucio to Vergilius' relationship with Charon, Vergilius saw through her attempts to goad him into unsteadiness and focused on dismantling Lucio during the battle rather than the Nursefather of the Thumb. Lucio suffered great injuries during this encounter, as while the threat to Charon's life was severely hampering Vergilius' opportunities and cool-headedness, the Red Gaze was still more than capable of ripping through them. When Valencina eventually received the news that the Dihui Star had retrieved the Golden Boughs from the HQ, she gave Charon back to Vergilius and departed with Lucio.
Later during Limbus Company's retaliative raid against the House of Spiders, Lucio was with his master in the Corridor of the Thumb. Vergilius, Rodion, Heathcliff, and Gregor eventually arrived, finding Lucio still injured and Valencina drunk. After some provocations from both sides, Valencina ordered Lucio to prepare for battle in spite of his injuries. Lucio proceeded to fight against the three Sinners while Valencina fought one-on-one against Vergilius; as the battle escalated, Vergilius and Valencina joined the others, and the Limbus Company team's strength begun to overwhelm the two.
When Lucio was wounded to the point where he could no longer fight, Valencina ordered him to continue attacking. The Sinners, recognizing that the youth needed urgent treatment, attempted to convince him to surrender rather than risk his life for someone who didn't value him. Despite this, Lucio continued onward, following Valencina's orders to attack Gregor, who had been growing unstable at the use of familiar phrases he'd once heard from his mother. After Lucio managed to land a hit on Gregor, the Sinner again warned him to back down, but Lucio marched ahead, and was run through by the surprise mutation of Gregor's bio-prosthetic arm, which ripped Lucio's heart out of his chest and killed him instantly.

---

## Marile

### Appearance
Marile appears to be a bulky man, though most of his features save for the top half of his face is covered. He has dark grey hair with white streaks (which are very inconspicuous under his hood). He has black eyes, and a stern facial expression. His mask is emblazoned with an orange circular shape, surrounded by three small rectangles logo. His uniform appears to have many layers, with a zipper running down its length and a white belt across his chest. A long dark brown coat is thrown over his uniform. The sleeves of his coat halt at the elbows and are tucked into long white gloves with two yellow belts. On his left sleeve, a dark red X has been crudely drawn over a logo similar to the one on his mask.
During combat, he wears a standard Lobotomy E.G.O::Red Sheet uniform, including a unique hood covered in the talismans worn on the outfit.

### Personality
Marile appears to be a blunt and serious work-aligned individual. He dislikes verbose people, seen by him attempting to silence Ran when they first invade the K Corp. headquarters. Another instance of this is when he retorts bluntly against Faust after her short exposition about "the new age". He is very adamant about pursuing his views, but he is shown to have some room for negotiation. He also arguably has his own kind of humor, evident from his comment about removing educational background from the Alliance recruitment requisites after Heathcliff says his piece about using force to convince people. He seems to have a meticulous hand, putting a lot of effort and care into creating the robots used by the terrorist group.

### Story
**Prior to Limbus Company***

Before the LCB arrived at K Corp. during the events of Canto IV, Marile and other members of the Technology Liberation Alliance had been involved in a number of terrorist attacks on the laboratories belonging to the Wing. Throughout those attacks, he had been working to develop machines capable of killing K Corp. employees in such a way that the healing ampules would be unable to restore them.
At some point in the past, Marile attended an interview for B Corp., where he was seen by Samjo.

**Canto IV: The Unchanging**

While the Sinners were on a tour of Dongrang's laboratory, the Alliance begins an attack on another lab in the building and the group rushed to the area. Here, they found Marile and Ran discussing the design of the machines they brought with them, as they were failing to do enough damage to the brain to prevent the healing ampules from functioning. When Ishmael called the two terrorists, Marile became upset as he disagrees with the idea that the Technology Liberation Alliance are a terrorist organization. Not long after, Shrenne arrived with reinforcements, the Fixers of Rosespanner Workshop. Upon seeing Niko and the other Fixers, Ran declared that this had become boring and tells Marile that they should leave, which he quickly agreed to.
The next time Marile encountered the Sinners is when he was surrounded by the bodies of K Corp. researchers who had been killed by the Alliance's machines. He had a short exchange with Faust and then Heathcliff where he elaborates on his motivation for being in the Technology Liberation Alliance. According to him, he and the other members had already cast aside the parts of the City's technology that they ideologically disagreed with and had no reason to care what would happen to the ignorant masses who would suffer with the loss of such progress. Because the people of City refused to believe in the truth even after seeing it with their own eyes, changing the world through force was the only remaining option. After this discussion, he engaged in a fight with the Sinners and was defeated.

---

## Matthias

### Appearance
Matthias is a bulky man, with dark skin and pure-white hair worn short with blunt bangs. He is typically seen wearing a pair of thick sunglasses, with a gold bridge between the lenses. He wears a white suit overtop a black dress shirt — unbuttoned and revealing a large scar on his chest — with a massive coat with the colors and pattern customary of members of the Middle worn over his shoulders. He keeps his Book of Vengeance on his left hip, with his opposite leg wrapped in golden chains. Notably, his right leg appears to shift through the use of his enhancement tattoos into a large claw, one he uses in combat. He is missing his right arm, though is shown to have worn white gloves on both hands in the past. His body is covered in enhancement tattoos, similar in design to other members of the Middle. On his back rests an oversized metallic sword and scabbard.
The sword, Lævateinn, is bound by at least three layers of seals, taking the form of thick chains keeping each layer tightly bound. When revealed, the sword appears with a thin-tipped appearance and a red burning hue across the entire length of the blade.

### Personality
Typical of those in his primary faction, Matthias is deeply devout to those on his side and brutal to those not. He is shown to feature an intense excitement at the possibility of reuniting with Ryōshū, who he called "buddy" in her youth. He features a toy-loving attitude, which contributes to a short attention span likened to hits destruction of new toys, as well as a tendency to buy and collect things he has no intention to actually use. Despite this somewhat immature personality, he remains highly capable in combat, able to fend off a variety of opponents at a time, with a litany of specific tools that assist his battles. Even with his boisterous personality, Matthias is a brutal and dedicated man who understands the goal of his side, never wavering when it is threatened or questioned.
However, at his core, Matthias is an intensely selfish man who only truly cares about short-term pleasure and indulging his hedonism. While he expresses affection for those under his watch, his understanding of parental care is highly superficial and neglectful, mostly involving flaunting his wealth and spoiling his "children" with no heed for consequences. Ultimately, he treats the needs of his peers as entirely irrelevant compared to his own, even fellow Middle members, and will even sacrifice them in a heartbeat if it benefits him.

### Story
**Prior to Limbus Company**

As a child, Matthias sought a toy of high acclaim, though was unable to purchase this item. Because of this failure, and the company's subsequent shutting-down, he experienced a deep feeling of despair being implanted to his being.
At some point, Matthias became a member of the Middle. During an expedition to the Ruins together with a Great Brother and Great Sister,[4] the group would discover the Lævateinn, a burning Relic of immense power. When the Great Brother claimed it as his own, Matthias, overtaken by envy, killed him and the Great Sister, destroying all evidence and claiming the sword as his own. Although Lævateinn was beyond his ability to wield to its full potential,[5] Matthias was nonetheless satisfied by simply being the owner of a legendary sword as he had once dreamed as a child, seeing his banishment as inconsequential in comparison. Despite this, his actions still aroused suspicion: though he held the rank of Great Brother, the members of the Syndicate were aware that he'd forsaken the absolute loyalty of the Middle.[6][3]
Among the five Fingers, Matthias was the Middle's representative in the process of raising Ryōshū into a "perfect blade". In her youth, Ryōshū was raised by Matthias, who frequently spoiled her with toys and violently punished those who slighted her.
At one point during Ryōshū's childhood, she attended a Ring subsidiary's art academy, where she got into a small scuffle with other children. She went home to Matthias and told him about the fight, causing him to praise her and leave the House of Spiders to enact vengeance on the class. Ryōshū came to class seeing that Matthias had beheaded her instructor and planned to take the right arms of several children, leaving her scarred and having her perspective on him changed.
He traveled with the girl, taking her out on streaks of buying expensive items, whether she wanted them or not, or taking her out to other Districts such as District 21.
During her rampage through the House of Spiders, Matthias was attacked by Ryōshū, having his right arm severed from his body. Despite the pain, all he did was question her reasoning, wondering if she were mad at him for something.
After Ryōshū's departure from the House of Spiders, Matthias adopted and began teaching an apprentice,[7] Kira, who shares similar interest in toys and battle as her "papa". During the time, the two bonded closely, though superfluously, with Kira's general quality of life being geared towards Matthias' interest in the easy-going and unsustainable. Matthias would become continually burdened by his debt to the Middle, though he appeared to remain close with Ricardo, who frequented the same salon as he and Kira.

**Canto IX: The Unsevering**

During the raid upon the Limbus Company HQ, Matthias was present in the assault, joined by his apprentice Kira who he told to not wander off, though she did regardless. In the beginning of the raid, Matthias was one of the first to begin the slaughter, witnessed by Marton as he launched his sword into members of the LCE.
Amidst the slaughter, Matthias was witnessed by members of the LCD, Ishmael, Outis, and Rodion, crushing members of the LCA that arrived to assist those trapped in the HQ. During his killings, Matthias repeatedly shouted "Yoshihide" in excitement. After his killings, he went to find where Kira, who was speaking to the LCD members and Sinners at the time, ran off to. In a moment of quick thinking, the Limbus Company employees managed to convince Kira into a game of hide and seek during the time they left Matthias to deal with one of the released Distortions, the Human Thunderbolt. While battling the Distortion, Matthias realized the group was the party responsible for the transgressions against Ricardo, who Matthias holds dearly in his heart.
After defeating the Distortion, Matthias traveled further into the facility, where Kira was being attacked by Drenched Gossypium, unable to free herself from the Abnormality's grasp. Despite the poor odds the girl had, Matthias instantly cleaved the Abnormality, causing it to revert to its egg form. Explaining his tendency to break new toys, Matthias began confronting the group, while the Sinners prepared to battle. At the necessary moment, however, the Sinners fell limp, leaving the LCD members to fend for themselves without assistance. This gave Moses and Ezra a moment to prepare another Abnormality, Ambling Pearl, which sprayed a paralytic acid and a load of flesh-eating maggots onto Matthias. Even still, Matthias swiftly defeated the Abnormality with two strikes, expressing his boredom at the stock of tricks and toys running low. While he prepared to finally end the LCD members, Moses utilized her E.G.O to temporarily cuff the man while Aeng-du and Ezra began an assault, with aims to behead the man. However, at this crucial moment, a Moonlight Stone Matthias held onto gave him enough leeway to begin moving again, allowing him to deflect the assault and severing Aeng-du's arms. Commending the girl for her arms' ability to remain holding her sword, he ensures a commendable death. In the few moments it took for him to prepare an attack against Moses, however, Vespa, newly appointed as a Color Fixer, managed to arrive on the scene and force Matthias into a deadlock.
During their stalemate, Matthias received the call to return to the House of Spiders, causing him to call off the fight with Vespa. Recognizing the need for both sides to tend to those important to them, he leaves the battle with Kira, letting Vespa know that he "appreciates a good bowl cut", in reference to the Fixer's hair.
Matthias and Kira are later encountered by Yi Sang, Don Quixote, Hong Lu, and the LCD amidst a massive storehouse in the House of Spiders, containing all of his boxed model toys. The two were watching shows on a television, where it's made known Matthias has allowed Kira to eat exclusively junk food for the last few days, despite the difficulties this may pose in raising a child. After a brief verbal standoff, the duo engaged the combined forces of Limbus Company in a battle. As Matthias began releasing more locks on Lævateinn to gain an upper hand, he was able to evade a decisive attack from Moses. While this happened, Kira vanished and pinned Vespa in a sneak attack, only for Matthias to brutally cleave her in half in order to land a clean hit on the Yellow Harpoon, claiming it to be a necessary sacrifice since the two were family. Disgusted by his callousness, Moses took the chance to line up a second attack that punched a hole through Matthias's torso, followed by Vespa cutting his head in half.

**Intervallo VII: Twining Threads**

Following Operation Spider Pyre, the House of Spiders was gradually traversed by the Sinners, accompanied by Kira and Alan of Wayfarer Company. The Middle's Corridor, now stripped of most of its goods and items, served as a sour reminder to Kira about her "papa"'s demise. While she desperately clung to her positive memories of the man, she was confronted by Ryōshū, who pushed her to acknowledge Matthias' inability to truly understand the interests of others ― and if he did ― destroy them.

### Trivia
Lævateinn, the Relic Matthias posseses, takes its name from a weapon created by the god Loki in Norse mythology.

---

## Moses

### Appearance
Moses is a short, middle aged woman with dark hair and white highlights, and visible wrinkles around her eyes. She has pale skin and dark grey eyes.
Her main outfit consist of a white shirt with long sleeves with ruffles, a red ribbon tied around the collar of her shirt and an off-the-sleeves grey jacket with golden trimming and cross-shapped golden buttons. She wears high waisted black pants with golden stripes, and black shoes with white and gold accents.
She always carries with her churchwarden pipe, later revealed to be her Psychoment, which has a long black mouthpiece and a golden diam, adorned with a red tassel. This allows her to purify incomplete Distortions, pacify and/or suppress enemies, depending on the smoke's color. Her "pale breath" attack comes at a direct cost of shortening Moses' lifespan. Her purple breath creates "binds" from her regret, her pale breath creates a blue mist capable of slowing down her opponent, her red breath transform the smoke into a blade, and her white breath creates a mist that protects from mental attacks.
After her conflict with Vespa during Chapter 19, her right arm was replaced by a prosthetic.

### Personality
Moses holds a calm and analytical attitude to any situations that she happens to find herself in, be it facing distortions or near-death scenarios. Even in moments of extreme danger, she is able to keep her composure and unravel the source of any distortions she happens to find herself against. She has a deep trust in her allies, especially her assistant Ezra, trusting in their combat capabilities and ability to stay safe while she utilizes her analytical skills.
She does not seem to have any aversion to shortening her own life-span if it means that it will protect either her or the people close to her, much to Ezra's dismay.
In the past, Moses was wholly devoted to Lady Dias as a result of being raised by her. Her entire sense of morality was based around what Dias wished for and what she did not, and Moses would do anything to help make Dias' dreams a reality. Through her time leading Udjat, Moses was ordered to commit horrible atrocities in the Smoke War and started to question herself, with this doubt in Dias coming to a head after Moses led vast majority of the Udjat to their deaths. After this event, Moses lost all faith in Dias and carries a deep sense of guilt over her actions that day. Due to this change in perspective, when speaking with Dias or Han Hee-joon, she takes on a much colder and aggressive attitude. Despite this, she tends to capitulate to their demands when offered a way to "atone for her past".

### Story
**Prior to The Distortion Detective***

Moses was an abandoned child who was found by Dias and raised by her. Dias told Moses to think of her as an older sister and gave her an education and a chance at life that Moses would never have had if not for Dias.[4] As Moses grew up, she found her entire worldview shaped by Dias' wishes and dreams, and was willing to follow her through anything to see her one day ascend to becoming the Head. When Dias formed the Udjat, she put Moses in the position of Captain and registered her as the Office Rep.[5]
During her time as the Captain of the Udjat, Moses did not treat her subordinates with much respect or regard their lives as having much value. She killed innocents and did not question Dias' orders even when she knew that she was being lied to. One day, Moses met Ezra, the 2,142nd agent of Udjat who was personally recommended by Lady Dias. Moses was not fond of the young, overconfident woman and the two got into a fight where Moses humiliated her in single combat. As the missions went on, however, Moses would start to see the members of Udjat as a sort of second family and grow closer to Ezra. Ezra questioned the actions they took, pointing out that as Fixers, killing innocents should be unthinkable to them, yet they did it anyways. This seed of doubt would grow in Moses, and truly shake her belief in Dias after the Smoke War began.
Dias started the Smoke War in order to help Lobotomy Corporation rise to be a Wing of the City, and sent the Udjat into frequent battles over the course of the war. During one of these battles, something went wrong and Moses quickly realized that she had just lead her entire Office to their deaths. In a desperate attempt to spare any of Udjat agents, she managed to save herself as well as Ezra and Han Hee-joon. This mission was some sort of experiment arranged by Dias, and Moses could no longer support the woman she had once been willing to do anything for. Around this point in time, Moses developed the ability to see Distortion on others and manifest her E.G.O.
Moses left Udjat along with Ezra and Han Hee-joon, and the three joined the Seven Association. Eventually Moses formed her own Office, which was affiliated with the Seven Association, and Ezra followed her and became her assistant. Now acting as the 'Distortion Detective', Moses' primary job was to help resolve cases of Distortion such as the ‘Merfolk’ and ‘Balloon People’. During the case of The Blood-red Night, Moses' Office assisted the other Offices in a collaborative effort to study her, although Moses and Ezra did little to contribute.
After several Distortion cases were resolved in the first several chapters, Han Hee-joon visited Moses' Office to deliver orders on behalf of the Seven Association. While Moses' Office is based in the Backstreets of District 14, he told them that in two months time they would need to take a WARP Train to District 11 to help with a case of Distortion. While not enthused about the order, Moses and Ezra agreed to it and decided to spend their remaining time in the District doing their usual contracts.
During this two month period, the two are attacked by a Syndicate who tried to buy — then take by force — Moses' smoking pipe. After defeating the thugs, they learn that they were hired by YuRia Atelier, who was interested in the pipe. Using Ezra's extensive knowledge of Workshops, they track down YuRia to her Atelier. After a brief fight with YuRia's sentient teddy bear assistants, they learn that she had recorded their fight with the Syndicate (which is a Taboo of N Corp.) and wishes to become Moses' assistant in order to be able to study her smoking pipe. YuRia was researching "Psychoments", her name for E.G.O, after developing one of her own and became interested in Moses' pipe as she realized its true power. Moses agreed to making YuRia her assistant, much to Ezra's confusion, and YuRia assisted them with their next case of Distortion.
During their contract with Tae-young Produce Company, Moses and the other two learned of the mysterious black boxes that can cause Distortions to manifest in people, before having to fight through multiple Distortions and nearly dying, with many things going wrong as they attempted to escape the building. While Ezra briefly distorted, Moses was able to bring her back to normalcy; among the damages, YuRia fell into a coma and transferred her consciousness into a teddy bear that Moses typically carried with her throughout the rest of the series. The contract was revealed to have had something to do with Dias, although they weren't able to learn more about how she was involved.
Due to YuRia's violation of N Corp.'s Taboo of filming within the District, the Grade 1 Fixer and Taboo Hunter of N Corp., Vespa Crabro, arrived at Moses' Office in order to inquire about the Taboo violator. Moses and Ezra lied to him about their involvement with YuRia as well as her whereabouts, and as soon as Vespa left, made plans to leave the District as soon as possible. They hired Dou Gui Combat Office to protect them, and solved the Distortion of the Office Rep's daughter in payment. After clashing with Vespa during their escape, during which Moses lost one of her arms, the three women eventually managed seal him in YuRia's workshop and take their WARP Train to District 11. Before they left, Ezra picked out a prosthetic arm for Moses to replace the one Vespa took from her.
In District 11, Moses and Ezra were told by Han Hee-joon that the Seven Association wanted them to investigate the strange Quercus Village, although this was later revealed to have been Dias' orders and he had lied to them. At the village, Moses noticed that none of the residents had any signs of Distortion, but they also did not have Psychoments. She soon learned that the village participated in a monthly ritual using a black box, similar to the one from the produce company, to draw out the Distortions from everyone present then transfer that Distortion into one person, who was then locked away in a cellar. Moses and Ezra, in their attempt to help that month's chosen sacrifice, followed the newly formed Distortion into the cellar where they were faced with the dozens of Distortions created over the past several years. Knowing they were outnumbered and had no way of escaping through normal means, Moses ordered YuRia to open her workshop and allow Vespa out. Vespa reluctantly assisted Moses and Ezra in subduing the Distortions and the four barely managed to make it out of the cellar alive.
After their escape from the cellar, the Udjat arrived and collected the surviving Distortions for Dias' collection, which is when Moses realized that Han Hee-joon had lied about the contract. Conveniently, Vespa was fired from his position as a Taboo Hunter by N Corp., meaning he no longer had a reason to fight Moses or Ezra. Han Hee-joon took Moses and her companions, now including Vespa, to one of Dias' mansions, where they learned the truth of her recent actions. Here, Dias expressed her want to hire Moses' Office to go to Nest L and collect Distortions for her. While Moses was at first reluctant, she soon saw it as a way to atone for her past and agreed to Dias' request. During this meeting, Dias also provided Moses with a new prosthetic arm, as she had broke her previous one in the cellar — a new prosthetic that could track her location and allow for easy communication between the parties.
Moses and her companions traveled to Nest L and quickly captured the Distortions 'The Laundry of Dreams' and 'The Human Thunderbolt', though were forced to withstand two waves of Sweepers after their car was damaged by the latter's powers. Attempting to escape the Sweepers, Moses knocked on several residential doors and was eventually allowed access into a home that was occupied by members of the Thumb. Moses negotiated with the Capo and agreed to retrieve some ammunition that had failed to be delivered to them in return for any information that the Thumb had on Distortions in the area. This led to the group meeting the Distortion 'The Marksman of the Mist', who had killed several members of the Zwei Association, as well as the Workshop Fixers who were tasked to make the Thumb's ammunition, with the situation growing even more complicated as a high grade Fixer working for the Zwei Association arrived to get revenge for his colleagues. Moses switched who amongst the Marksman, the Zwei Fixer, and the Thumb that she sided with several times amidst the confrontation, with ultimately the Distortion and the Thumb dying and the Fixer walking away.

***Limbus Company***

Moses, Ezra, and Vespa ultimately found themselves working for Limbus Company's Distortion Department, with Moses as the team's On-site Investigative Reasoning Team Leader. During the events of Intervallo III: Yield My Flesh to Claim Their Bones, Ezra reported to Moses on Dante's success in turning off the Monolith. She later wrote a report that was sent to the Sinners regarding the company's classifications of Distortions.

**Canto VII: The Dream Ending**

Moses and Ezra both provided intel to the LCB regarding Bloodfiends during their Golden Bough retrieval mission in La Manchaland. While unable to appear in person due to "personal reasons", Moses informed the Sinners of all of the knowledge she has gathered about the nature of Bloodfiends and their relationship to Distortions. At the end of the call, Moses expressed a desire to one day meet with Dante and shared that she is glad to know that there was another person who is able to sense Distortions like she can.

**Canto IX: The Unsevering**

Moses, Ezra, and the recently recruited Aeng-du went to Limbus Company's headquarters to sit in on a presentation done by the LCE department regarding the Golden Boughs. Before the presentation could begin, the HQ was raided by members of each of the Five Fingers who belonged to the House of Spiders and the entire facility turned to chaos. The three women, as well as Hohenheim and Marton of the LCE department, managed to lock themselves in the LCE research team's broadcast sector where they were safe from the escaped Distortions and Abnormalities that were let loose by the Fingers. The Sinners of the LCB eventually found themselves at the room and, after some confusion on if they were allies or foes, the two groups united to discuss how to reclaim the facility from the invading Syndicate members and protect the Golden Boughs being stored there.
The plan they decided on was to split up into three groups, with the LCD handling the suppression of the Abnormalities, Distortions, and Peccatula roaming the halls so that reinforcements would be able to reach critical areas faster once they arrived. Things immediately did not go as planned, however, as before they were able to split up in their designated teams, walls dropped down separating the Sinners that forced them to join the other groups. Now with Outis, Rodion, Hong Lu, and Ishmael working with them, the LCD set off on their mission and soon ran into the Middle Nursefather Matthias and his apprentice Kira.
The group ran from the two members of the Middle, but Kira chased after them and Matthias quickly caught up with them after finishing taking care of the LCA agents that had attacked him. Moses decided to let the Human Thunderbolt, who had been contained in the HQ, attack their foes for a distraction, and the Distortion reanimated the corpses of the LCA agents to swam the two while the group made their escape. Kira continued hunting them down, treating it like a game of hide and seek, and Moses came up with a plan to distract Kira by forcing her to fight the Abnormality Drenched Gossypium. This worked successfully, with Kira treating the battle like a video game boss fight, but fell apart when Matthias arrived to protect his daughter and suppressed the Abnormality.
Thinking quickly, Moses then decided to let Ambling Pearl fight with Matthias in the hopes that its paralyzing, corrosive attacks would stall him, but he defeated it in a single blow before it could do any significant damage. Moses used her violet breath to restrain him while Ezra and Aeng-du launched a team attack, but Matthias countered the attack with ease, and freed himself of the violet bindings using one of M Corp.'s Moonlight Stones. Although all of these clever tricks had winded Matthias, he was still more than capable of fighting and decided it was time to finish off the injured members of the LCD. Before his attack against Moses could land, however, Vespa, who had returned from finishing the paperwork to become a Color Fixer, arrived just in time to block it and fend Matthias off. Not long after, the House of Spiders received the order to retreat, and Matthias and Kira left, with all members of Moses' group managing to survive.
Later, the surviving members of Limbus Company decided to launch a counter-raid on the House of Spiders in order to retrieve the Golden Boughs that had been stolen from them. Moses and the members of the LCD planned to participate in the counter-raid, excluding Aeng-du who was still recovering from her injuries during the raid.
The LCD, alongside Don Quixote, Hong Lu and Yi Sang entered the Middle's Corridor within the House. The group engaged in battle with Matthias and Kira. Moses utilized her smoking pipe during the fight, providing support for her teammates. To finish the fight, Moses generates a powerful attack known as the Crimson Point. She misses with her first Crimson Point, but scores a direct hit with her second on Matthias, mortally wounding him. Vespa finishes off Matthias by slicing through his head. The battle ends with Matthias dead, and with Kira apprehended.

### Trivia
Moses' name is taken from the prophet Moses.
Of the Five Fingers, Moses seems to like the Index the least, as she finds interacting with its members to be like talking to a brick wall.
Moses' hand-on-chin pose used to have an error in its sprite, with an additional prosthetic hand being visible from under her coat. This was addressed in the January 8th, 2026 update.
The ID card she wears has a picture of YuRia in her teddy bear form on Moses' shoulder rather than a picture of Moses herself.

---

## Nelly

### Appearance
Nelly is an olive-skinned woman with long brown hair and golden-brown eyes. In her first appearance in Canto VI, she wears the uniform common of the female Edgar Family Butlers, consisting of an ankle-length black dress and a white apron. Her dress is decorated with a silver crest at the collar, and her hair is tied in a high ponytail and adorned by a frilly white headband.
After joining the New League of Nine Littérateurs, Nelly appears with her hair down, donning a blue headband tied with a red ribbon, and she wears an N Corp. uniform consisting of a long dark blue coat with red detailing with a matching skirt and vest, over a white shirt with a red ribbon at her neck. She also wears black gloves and an ammunition belt.
Nelly is always seen carrying a large brown suitcase slung over her right shoulder, where she carries her combat cutlery.

### Personality
An extremely competent high-ranking Fixer in service of the Edgar family, Nelly is initially shown to be a very kind and understanding ally to the Sinners, accompanying them around Wuthering Heights as a guide. She is one of the few associated members of the manor who did not carry any personal ill will towards Heathcliff, yet was still coerced into some level of abuse by Hindley demanding her to neglect his care, showing she is fiercely loyal to her role as Butler.
Nelly is later revealed to have lied to the Sinners, having been not only completely aware of all the events that had transpired at the manor after Heathcliff's departure, but having been a catalyst for many of them. Having received a mirror from Hermann that showed her the possibilities of the Mirror Worlds, Nelly grew scared of suffering the same fate as her other selves, suffering due to the fall-out of Catherine and Heathcliff and being unable to live for herself. This caused her to grow bitter and resentful towards the world around her, eventually teaming up with the N Corp. Director to spur Catherine's death wish and supporting her in the creation of the laboratory.
Despite the resentment that lead her to conspire with Hermann, Nelly claims to carry no ill will towards Heathcliff and Catherine, fondly recalling the two's childhood and wishing for Heathcliff to know her actions are dictated not by contempt, but by her desire to be free and live the life she wishes. All through the events at Wuthering Heights, Nelly mantains a calm and polite demeanor with him and the Sinners, only truly breaking down when recalling the sorrow she saw through the Mirror.

### Story
**Prior to Limbus Company***

Nelly had served Wuthering Heights for the majority of her life, as she was already a Fixer when Heathcliff first arrived to the manor, when he, Catherine and Hindley were still young.
Nelly describes herself as Catherine and Heathcliff's nanny, having been their main caretaker during their youth. She is often shown to be taking care of the children, making sure they went to sleep on time, comforting Catherine when she would complain of a ghost haunting the manor, and lecturing the children when they misbehaved and left the house without permission.
Nelly was Catherine's confidant, and was the person Catherine discussed her to marry Linton rather than Heathcliff with, a conversation that would lead Heathcliff to run away from the manor. Following Heathcliff's departure, Nelly took care of Catherine as her health deteriorated.
At a point, Nelly encountered Hermann, who gifted her a Mirror shard: by gazing into it, Nelly witnessed countless Mirror Worlds, which caused a great despair to take root in her as she realized she would likely remain caught in the crossfire of Heathcliff and Cathy's relationship no matter what world. This led Nelly to gift the Mirror to Catherine, kickstarting the events that would lead to the experiment through which Catherine meant to erase herself, an action that would free all versions of Nelly.
During this time, Nelly would burn the letters Heathcliff sent Catherine, severing the possibility for the two to reconnect, and leading instead Catherine to marry Linton, which would give her the financial means to create the laboratory beneath Wuthering Heights. After the two's marriage, Nelly took up the role of Chief Butler of the Edgar family, and kept assisting N Corp. in their summoning of Erlking Heathcliff, whom she would use to help Catherine acquire the manor from Hindley.
Nelly kept helping in the development of the laboratory up until Catherine was sealed in her coffin, after which she would send the inviting Heathcliff back to the manor.

**Canto VI: The Heartbreaking**

Nelly was the one to first welcome the Sinners into Wuthering Heights, ushering them inside and guiding the group to the central hall for the reading of Catherine's will. She was the one to break the news to Heathcliff that Catherine was dead, after which she had to subdue him for obstructing the Öufi Association as they attempted to commence the reading. During a discussion on Butlers, Nelly mentioned the details of her contract, which tied her to only Catherine, and did not extend to Linton. After Heathcliff reawakened, she informed him of the situation the manor went through following his departure, until the first strike of lightning hit the manor, causing a temporary power outage.
Once the power returned to the building, Nelly and the Sinners were transported to a corridor within the building suddenly. Nelly led the Sinners as they attempted to navigate the transfigurated manor, warning them to watch out for the Dead Rabbits members, commenting on their red eyes. Nelly and Heathcliff discussed the state of depression Catherine fell after his departure, with Nelly appearing confused at Heathcliff's question on whether she'd gotten his letters, and replying they'd never received any. The group then reached the late lady's room and recovered her diary, which led them to the fireplace and into the basement.
Upon descending into the laboratory, Nelly immediately recognized the Golden Bough within the coffin housing Catherine, pointing it out to the group. After combat ensued with Hindley, the Dead Rabbits, and the Ring scientists that manned the laboratory, and after Linton's corpse was utilized for the summoning of Erlking Heathcliff, the Identity took Catherine's coffin and fled to the rooftop, with Nelly following the Sinners as they gave chase.
While attempting to catch up to him, Nelly questioned Heathcliff if he, or any of the Sinners, understood the importance of the Golden Boughs at all, upon which she was brushed off by Heathcliff, who marched on relentlessly. Nelly stood behind as the group managed to reach Erlking Heathcliff thanks to Dante's newly developed abilities, and as Meursault restrained the man using his Chains of Others E.G.O. While the group debated on what could have been the cause for Catherine's interest in Mirror Technology, Outis pointed out that Nelly appeared to know far more than she had let on, having recognized the Dead Rabbits' eyes and having an amount of knowledge of the Golden Boughs. Right as she was exposed as a traitor, Nelly released Erlking Heathcliff from his binds, defending him as he traveled to the manor rooftop. Nelly attempted to buy time for Erlking Heathcliff by fighting against the Sinners, but she was defeated. At this point, Nelly revealed the fear that she had felt upon seeing into the Mirror Worlds, explaining her actions had been for the sake of breaking out of the shackle of Catherine and Heathcliff, who had bound and limited her freedom in so many worlds.
Nelly made one last attempt to stop Heathcliff from progressing by revealing herself to have been the one to burn his letters before they reached Catherine. Shocked by the betrayal, Heathcliff suddenly disappeared on the spot, goaded on by Nelly claiming that he'd returned to the Backstreets where he belonged. Heathcliff was then helped out of his state by Dante and Catherine's intervention, and once returned, being aware he'd inherited the estate after Linton and Hindley's deaths, he declared Nelly free of her contract and asked her to do as she would with her life. As he and the Sinners proceeded to the rooftop, Nelly began sobbing.
Nelly would not return until after the death of Erlking Heathcliff and erasure of Catherine, at which point she swept in and secured the Golden Bough from the rooftop. Nelly declared that she would take it to Hermann, to which Heathcliff replied he'd eventually get his Bough and Catherine back. By this point, Nelly no longer had any knowledge of that name, and she simply commented by reminding Heathcliff the Boughs may make any dream come true, before leaving.

**Canto VIII: The Surrendered Witnessing**

Now an official member of the New League of Nine Littérateurs, Nelly reached Hongyuan following the end of the second round of the Daguanyuan Family Hierarch Evaluations as the various factions assemble to aid their preferred candidates. After retrieving the Family Hierarch Anamnaworm, the Xianhuang Worm, from the Tiekan Temple, Jia Huan and Gubo escaped Daguanyuan through a route secured by a secondary team led by Nelly.

**Canto IX: The Unsevering**

Following the raid of the House of Spiders, Nelly was shown upon her return to N Corp., as she relayed to Hermann the events of the Limbus Company mission at the House. Hermann commended Nelly on her investigative abilities, and the various members of the New League briefly discussed the future plans of N Corp. As the rest of the New League went to join the upcoming board meeting, Nelly departed, returning to her task of observing the LCB.

### Trivia
Nelly is based on Ellen "Nelly" Dean from *Wuthering Heights*, the housekeeper at Wuthering Heights who follows Catherine Earnshaw after her marriage, as well as the nanny of both Catherine Linton and Hareton Earnshaw.
Nelly's literary counterpart is the main narrator of the story of *Wuthering Heights*, having witnessed much of Heathcliff's youth at the manor and his relationship to Catherine, and recounting it to the current tenant of Thrushcross Grange. Nelly shows herself to be alternatively fond or resentful of the members of the Earnshaw family and Heathcliff, and appears to never have married or have much of a tale of her own to tell, outside of the events she witnessed at the Earnshaw and Linton households. This concept is reflected and taken to its extreme in *Limbus Company*, where Nelly becomes terrified by the idea of her life constantly playing out with her serving as only a minor character in other people's lives, and seeks to free herself from her role as a mere narrator.
This is possibly referenced in the Abnormality Portrait of a Certain Day.
Nelly's manipulation of the letters as seen during the Canto is directly inspired by her literary basis: during the first half of the novel, Nelly is forced by Heathcliff to give the dying Catherine his letter where he requests to meet her again, while in the second half, Nelly is the one who burns Catherine Linton's correspondence with Linton Heathcliff, much to the chagrin of the girl.
A Mirror World version of Nelly appears during Erlking Heathcliff's backstory. This version of Nelly appears to be incredibly similar to her, with no visible changes apparent.

---

## Night Drifter

### Appearance
The Night Drifter is an elderly man with long gray hair tied behind his head, and a similarly gray beard on his chin, curling at the end. He wears a dingy straw hat with two hanging straps, as well as a large green scarf around his neck. Beneath this scarf, he wears a brown-and-gray hanfu, tied at the waist by a dark sash and ropes. His feet are wrapped in gray cloth, connected to similarly gray soles. He is seen wielding a wooden staff with a single leaf at its top, as well as a large orange drinking gourd with a small yellow sash tied at its middle.

### Personality
The Night Drifter is a highly capable man, reacting laxly while carrying out his assassin work, confident he will succeed. He has a penchant for drinking, which allows for him to better handle his opponents. Like most of those working in line of the familial battles within Daguanyuan, he has little moral qualms with attacking unwilling combatants when ordered to.
He reveals a more moral side during the events of Intervallo VI, having once been a father so wrought by the grief of losing his daughter that he chose to abandon his entire life of notoriety. He views Jia Xichun with a level of grief, saddened in being tasked with killing one of his two final disciples.

### Story
**Prior to Limbus Company***

Once a formidable blade fiend recognized for his skills, the Night Drifter was given the title of one of the Ten Blades of the East. With this immense title and skill, he was feared for his work among Syndicates. However, he would have to bury his daughter who passed during one of Hongyuan's restructuring days, which completely altered the man's view of life.
Wrought with the grief of this event, he chose to forever abandon the use of his blades and instead live as a drunken stranger who abandoned both his name and life.

**Canto VIII: The Surrendered Witnessing**

Following the first round of the Family Hierarch Evaluations, Hong Lu and the Sinners returned to Baoyu's residence. Here, the Night Drifter, alongside a gang of podao-wielding assassins, broke into the residency through the roof. While the Sinners were capable of fending off several of the assassins, the Night Drifter joined the scuffle. Despite Outis attempting to gleam information from the man, he simply states that he has no name yet is known by others as the Night Drifter. Easily dispatching several of the Sinners, the Night Drifter crushes the brain of Hong Lu, lamenting that the victim may have been as skilled as himself, had Hong Lu been trained under his tutelage. Believing his job to be done, the Night Drifter, alongside the remaining assassins, then disappeared into the darkness.
He is later mentioned to have been among the assassins hired by the mother of Xue Baochai, looking to eliminate Hong Lu.

**Intervallo VI: Spring Cultivation**

Amidst the training of Jia Xichun and Sinclair, the Night Drifter was covertly hired by Jia Yuanchun who looked to assassinate the rising Hierarch. However, caught between emotions, Night Drifter instead chose to train the two; even if he were to attempt an assassination, he chose to sell the wolfsbane he was given to buy several expensive wines. During the month of training, Night Drifter diligently trained his disciples.
At the conclusion of the tests, Jia Xichun was kidnapped per the order of Jia Yuanchun, who aimed to kill the Hierarch. The Night Drifter remained responsible for the killing, being her executioner that challenged her to a final duel. This duel was quickly interrupted by both the Sinners arriving and the Heishou Pack's Si branch. Annoyed by the interference, the Night Drifter was incidentally stuck by one of the Si branch members that aimed to kill Xichun, poisoning him. Despite this, he continued the final battle, proclaiming that it would be bad news for Hongyuan if she allowed him to live. In their final battle, he was struck down and killed by Jia Xichun, marking his final lesson to his disciples. Depending if Jia Xichun's level is raised high enough, he either succumbs to the poison first, or is struck down by the Hierarch's skills.
His true identity as an assassin of Jia Yuanchun was ultimately covered up, with the man ending up buried in an unmarked grave and being swept under the rug as a random deranged attacker.

### Trivia
The Night Drifter's fighting style emulates the Chinese martial art of the Drunken Fist style.
Drunken Fist's first written reference is believed to have been in Water Margin, one of the four most prominent pieces of classic Chinese novels. In *Water Margin*, the Drunken Fist style is used by Wu Song, one of the 108 Heroes and the Tianshang Star.
The Night Drifter teaches Xichun and Sinclair the concept of Taoism, a Wu wei.
The Night Drifter's teaching of Emptying sound(无音), Emptying mind(无念), Emptying form(无形) from Intervallo 8.5-4 is a reference to the concept of Taoism. This is a form of "letting go of egoistic concerns" or "Emptying the mind".

---

## Niko

### Appearance
Niko appears to be an older man, with a noticeable amount of wrinkles on his face. His graying hair is parted, with the red tips of it pointing upwards. He wears bronze, diamond-shaped earrings on both ears and a black choker. On his shoulders, he wears a rose red jacket that has bronze trimming and a large Rosespanner decal on the right edge. Beneath, he wears a pale purple dress shirt, with a strap that crosses his chest perpendicularly. Along with this, he wears dark pants and heels on his lower half. His weapon is proudly displayed on his back, resembling a large hybrid of a wrench and chainsaw.

### Personality
Initially, Niko shows an aloof and confident personality, happily chatting with the Sinners about gambling in J Corp. However, once Shrenne's scheme is found out, Niko is shown to be much more confrontational and defensive, though still expressing an innate aloofness, such as declaring a timeout whilst fighting the Sinners. He is primarily driven by greed, as seen by his sole reason for taking Shrenne's deal being the money rewarded for taking the contract.

### Story
Prior to the events of Canto IV, Niko, and by proxy, the Rosespanner Workshop, were hired by Shrenne to protect the group traveling in K Corp., though on the stipulation of eliminating Dongrang and the Sinners in secrecy.
Upon first arriving, he joked that Ran and Marile being intimidated by their arrival was the cause for the Technology Liberation Alliance fleeing. From this point, he and the Rosespanner Workshop accompany Dongrang's group, happily chatting with Rodion and Heathcliff about supposed secrets of the gambling done in J Corp. Niko stood back until the group arrived within the Lobotomy Corporation Branch located within K Corp.'s Nest, at which point he became defensive over the group's general discussion about his and Shrenne's actions, something which they noticed to be suspicious. After a short battle, Niko called for a timeout as one of his Workshop's members reminded him not to use any of the Ampoules, to which Niko criticized this man for breaching the secret contract between the group and their employers. With a complaint that he should have gambled more the day prior had he known he would be fighting, Niko resumed combat with the Sinners and was ultimately killed.

---

## Old G Corp Head Manager

### Appearance
The Old G Corp. Head Manager is a burly man with a large insectile head, brown in color. He has an eyeless face with a variety of grooves across the surface, resembling carapace, which travels upwards into two tall, inward pointing, horns. He has a set of pincers surrounding a set of human teeth, a remnant of him pre-augmentation. He wears a gray-blue army uniform with a coat resting over his shoulders, covered in dried blood. He wears a large silver belt on his waist, his sprite showing him holding this belt with bloodied hands. His pants are tucked into boots stitched down the front.

### Personality
The Old G Corp. Head Manager views himself as an honorable soldier and he still cares about his subordinates even after the end of the war. He is resentful of Gregor for becoming a deserter and blames him for abandoning his comrades after being such an important figure for the Wing. Despite a decade passing since The Smoke War concluded, he feels as if he has never escaped the battlefield and views the desperate things he has done after the war to keep himself and his fellow veterans alive as disgusting, thinking of himself and the other veterans as no more than pests.

### Story
**Prior to Limbus Company***

The Old G Corp. Head Manager was once a proud soldier of G Corp. during the time of The Smoke War. He served alongside Gregor as the Head Manager of his unit, before Gregor deserted. Since the end of the war, he has continued to act as a leader for the remaining soldiers who had served under him.

**Canto I: The Outcast**

The LCB met the Old G Corp. Head Manager in Branch D-02, where he is one of many members of Old G Corp. who have grouped together to scavenge the old Lobotomy Corporation facility for Enkephalin and other highly valued items. He recognized Gregor immediately upon seeing him and confronted him over how he had deserted G Corp. when they needed him, only to now be killing his former comrades. When Gregor tells him the war has ended over a decade ago, the Head Manager disagreed and says that nothing ever ends and that they are still fighting every day, to which Gregor reluctantly admitted that he understands. He then simply stated that there is only one verdict that awaits deserters and attacked. After the battle, he warned the group to not proceed further before he takes his final breath and dies.
While his actual self remains dead, a recollected version of the Old G Corp. Head Manager appears in Gregor's fathoms.

---

## Panther

### Appearance
Panther is an average height, lean man with tanned skin and dark black hair cut just before his shoulders. Panther has dark grey, almost black eyes and sports black facial hair as well. He wears a single, purple earring on his left ear in the shape of a twisting snake. His outfit consists of a black hooded sheepskin cloak, held in the middle by a grey belt. The cloak has silver buckled pockets and grey wool trim on the hood, sleeves and in a thin stripe down the middle of the cloak. He wears black and grey buckled boots. The cloak is worn over a black turtleneck. Panther also wields a silver, double-sided halberd with gold edges on the blades and a purple tassel tied to the spear end of the weapon.

### Personality
Panther is a rational and observational person, being the one to focus the discussion on what information they could gather. He can also be cruel, as seen by his comment on wanting to see Dante's expression while they died and his remark on the Sinners being so weak that they are no fun to kill. Despite this, he is not overconfident, retreating when told to.

### Story
Panther, Lion, and Wolf are met just as they corner Dante in a dark forest as a part of a plan made by their master. They decided to kill them once they realize that, thanks to Dante's new head, they will be unable to get any information out of them. While Lion wanted to draw it out, both Panther and Wolf agree it would be best to kill them quickly. Just as Wolf was about to kill Dante, they heard a noise, realizing that a bus was heading towards them. The Sinners exited the bus and engage the three in a fight, but Panther and his companions made short work of them and are only stopped when Vergilius dismembers Wolf and Lion and orders Panther to drag them away in a retreat.

### Trivia
Panther, Lion and Wolf are based on the three beasts from the first Canto of Dante's Inferno, which symbolize the three major divisions of the sins punished in hell. The panther, the first beast encountered by Dante, is believed to represent fraud and malice, and particularly the deadly sins of envy and lust.
Though their master is currently unknown, Vergilius referring to them as "the Serpent", as well as the presence of purple snake ornaments on all three group members, it is possible the identity of the master is none other than Iori, the Purple Tear.

---

## Paula

### Appearance
Paula is a tall woman with a pale complexion. She has short light brown hair parted in the middle, and round light brown eyes. She wears the uniform of the Zwei Association Western Branch, consisting of a suit of white metal armor over a yellow shirt and blue tabard, and a long blue cape. She can be seen carrying the standard-issued Zwei West greatsword.
Following her Corrosion at the hands of E.G.O gear, her armor is bloodied and pierced by several blooming roses that wrap along her body, blossoming as it feeds on blood. Most notably, the largest rose blooms from the top of her head.

### Personality
Paula is a rational and reserved Fixer, focused on her mission. In contrast to her partner Camille, Paula prefers to stay quiet in most situations, only speaking when asked or to find details about her mission.

### Story
Paula first appeared when the Sinners arrive at the Fixer conference in the District 16 Backstreets, being one of the numerous parties assigned to the mission, along with her work associate Camille. After the details of La Manchaland were explained, the pair elaborated that they are on a recovery contract for a specific "guest" at the park, and are aiming to minimize their time there. To Don Quixote’s disapproval, Paula revealed that there are no plans to rescue every stranded person in La Manchaland, sparking a disagreement between Don Quixote and Camille.
Discovered further into the Lobotomy Corporation branch within La Manchaland, it was found that the two Corroded while donning E.G.O gear extracted from the Four-hundred Roses Abnormality. Meursault notes the likelihood the two used the gear in a final gambit of survival that ultimately did not succeed. Now mindless due to the Corrosion, the two battled the Sinners and were ultimately put down in the battle.

### Trivia
Paula, as the Budding Zwei Fixer, is fought in the Canto VII Dungeon, The Tale of a Great Fixer Who Once Reached for The Dream. Despite the enemy sprite not matching correctly with her armor and featuring a reused Yurodivy enemy head, she and Camille are identified by the Sinners within the text, meaning the Budding Zwei Fixer is still intended to be Paula, and the sprite's appearance is likely only incorrect due to time constraints.
Zwei Association West Section concept art showcasing two Zwei West Fixers
Paula's design appears to be directly based, if not outright taken, from the Zwei Association West Section concept art shown during Project Moon's July 2024 update schedule livestream (timestamp around 31:52). In that concept art, two Zwei West Fixers could be seen, with the left one having a practically identical hairstyle and armor design to that of Paula's.

---

## Pilot

### Appearance
Pilot is a man with a youthful appearance, light brown skin and curly brown hair. He has deep brown eyes, with three circular marks in a horizontal pattern beneath the right one. He sports the LCCB uniform, consisting of a turquoise shirt and matching trousers, and a vest to which a communication device is attached. On his left earlobe, he has a small silver piercing.

### Personality
Pilot is an enthusiastic employee who takes pride in his job and holds deep admiration for his teammates as well as the members of the LCB. As the rookie of the team, he lacks the experience and knowledge that would be expected of an LCCB member and is naïve to many of the situations that he encounters on the job, sometimes making mistakes that brings great risk to the LCB. Even still, he values his work and tries his best to improve himself to be of greater use to the company.

### Story
**Canto V: The Evil Defining**

As a member of the Before Team, Pilot joined the mission to travel to U Corp.'s Lobotomy Corp. Branch and survey it in search of the Golden Bough. Shortly finding the Bough, the team was attacked by the Twinhook Pirates, accompanied by members of the Middle, among which was the Big Brother Ricardo. Pilot's team leader, Haru, managed to convince the assailants that the team was actually led by Pilot, leading them to capture him, while the rest of the team remained trapped within the Branch as it was consumed by the Pallid Whale.
Pilot was then imprisoned in a storage container, and later freed by the LCB. Pilot delivered a message from Saude to the Sinners, revealing her to be still alive following the events of Canto III. At this point, he recounted of the team's encounter with the Twinhook Pirates and the Middle, and produced a hidden paper where he'd marked down the coordinates of the Lobotomy Corp. Branch. Pilot requested to join the Sinners on the mission, although Dante declined his offer as to not endanger him. During the interaction with the LCB, Pilot eventually started breaking down and mourning his team, and was comforted by the Sinners before they departed to complete their mission.

**Intervallo V: Nocturnal Sweeping**

Some time prior to the Sinners' arrival at H Corp., Pilot would be tasked with finding a person connected to the Jia family in preparation for the LCB's future operations in the area. He was then approached by Qingtao, a former servant of the family. As the Sinners reached the District 8 Backstreets, Pilot, together with Saude, met up with them, and Pilot presented Qingtao to the Sinners as their guide through the Backstreets.
After the major events of the Intervallo, he appeared again with Saude to apologize for his mistake.

**Canto VIII: The Surrendered Witnessing**

At the start of the Canto, Pilot and Saude accompanied the Sinners and Jia Xichun's faction as they awaited the palanquins that would take them to Daguanyuan for H Corp.'s Family Hierarch evaluations. While Saude boarded the palanquin with the Sinners, Pilot stayed behind, informing Dante that he would have work to do outside of Daguanyuan.

**Canto IX: The Unsevering**

Following the conclusion of Vergilius' separate travels, Pilot, who accompanied the man for an unknown portion of its time, was caught in the attack led by Valencina and her apprentice. While he remained in critical state, he managed to survive the attack. Following the conclusion of the House of Spiders' raid on Limbus Company HQ, he was among the injured given treatment via ampules.

### Trivia
Similar to how Effie and Saude's names are homophonic to "episode" when combined, Pilot's name may be a reference to pilot episodes.

---

## Pip

### Appearance
Pip is a young boy with dark skin and ginger, shaggy hair. He has large green eyes and freckles across his nose, He wears a large, green, button-up shirt with several tears and stitches across it. The oversized sleeves are rolled up to reveal an olive underside. His pants are similar to his top, with the pantlegs rolled up to his calves with bare feet.
During Canto V, he wears the same clothes, yet is now seen with the Pallidifaction caused by the Pallid Whale, and sporting a deranged expression with his left eye covered.

### Personality
Pip has a young personality, being generally emotional and rambunctious, yet he appears to have a great level of self sufficiency due to his role on The Pequod, something most seasoned sailors struggled with. By the time of Canto V, he later developed a rabid and dark personality, seemingly developed by his time around Ahab and her manipulation, spurring him to even kill other crew members, motivated by his past friendship with Stubb.
He has a habit of speaking in the third person.

### Story
**Prior to Limbus Company***

At some point, Pip joined the Pequod as a crew member, becoming a member of Ahab's hunt of the Pallid Whale. He would grow close with those of the crew, and especially Stubb.
Through the Golden Bough's resonance, it was shown that Pip dreamed of becoming a landlord once the hunt was done, in hopes of making a lot of money, causing a friendly session of teasing between he and Starbuck. During a later confrontation with the Pallid Whale, Stubb was bit whilst defending Pip, causing Ahab to give Stubb a final farewell, motivating Pip and the rest of the crew to continue on, using the newly formed Mermaid as a compass to the Whale. Even later, Pip ended up having to go and manage the Mermaid locked away in the ship, something which was comforted and explained by Starbuck and Ahab respectively. He would be apart of the inevitable confrontation of the Pallid Whale, and be consumed with the rest of the crew, beginning their Pallidification.

**Canto V: The Evil Defining**

While in Pequod Town, he closely worked with Ahab and the rest of the crew. When the plan to kill the Whale begins, he accompanied the majority of the crew, while Queequeg would join the LCB Sinners travelling along another path. During this time, Pip became a part of the group that gradually culled the horde of sailors with them, spurred by Ahab. At the arrival of the group, the Sinners faced off against Ahab, and Pip would be consumed by her E.G.O, Gasharpoon, and used as fuel alike the rest of his remaining crew.

### Trivia
Pip's namesake comes from Herman Melville's Moby-Dick: he shares his name Pippin, Pip for short, the cabin-boy from the novel.
In the course of the novel, Pip is forced to replace a crewmate on Stubb's boat, and falls into the water during the hunt, only being found by the Pequod and saved by chance. Pip is traumatized by the experience, and is considered mad by the other members of the crew; Ahab then takes pity on him, and takes the youth under his wing. This is reflected in Pip's delirium towards the end of Canto V, in which Ahab's own madness overtakes Pip, and he appears overjoyed at the prospect of slaying the Whale.

---

## Queequeg

### Appearance
Queequeg is a well-built, muscular woman with dark complexion. She has dark brown hair worn in thick braids that reach down to her chest, and that she decorates with golden cuffs. Her most notable feature is the tattoo enhancements from the Middle, broken up by extensive, self-inflicted scarring visible across her entire upper body and head. Queequeg wears a sleeveless, mud-green shirt underneath a heavy gray vest and thick green pants tucked into boots, as well as two golden bands around her upper arms. As a harpooneer, she also has thick brown ropes tied around her upper and lower arms, midsection, waist, right calf and left ankle. These ropes are also used to securely tie a short harpoon to her left forearm.
During her time in Pequod Town, Queequeg was covered in a pallidification membrane and wore a crude metal mask that only showed her left eye, which appeared wide and frenzied.

### Personality
Queequeg is a quiet and slow-talking woman with a generally blunt and stoic way of thinking. Queequeg carries heavy guilt over her actions during her old life as a member of the Middle, and is so strongly driven in her will to remove this stain in her past that she is willing to go to any length to find atonement, harming herself with the goal of removing the mark of the Syndicate and devoting herself completely to her work as a harpooneer for Ahab's crew. In her time on The Pequod, Queequeg grew to greatly value her crewmates, and particularly treasuring her bond with Ishmael, with the two dreaming of starting a new life together after the end of the voyage. Her devotion to Ahab would never falter after the destruction of the ship, with Queequeg believing Ahab's claim that at the end of the voyage "everything would come to be", and hoping to one day see the surface, as well as Ishmael, for a last time.

### Story
**Prior to Limbus Company***

Queequeg was originally a member of The Middle, having spent many years working under the Syndicate, to the point of receiving the rank of Big Sister. At a point, Queequeg began to hate the violent life she'd been leading, and decided to leave The Middle and start anew: to effectively cut her allegiance, she had to mutilate her tattooed skin, tongue and brain.
After becoming a crew member aboard the Pequod, she became very close friends with Ishmael, with whom she shared a room. During the voyage, Queequeg started building a coffin for herself, so that in the event of her death, her body would be safe from the Whales and Mermaids. She went missing, together with the Pequod's crew, during the shipwreck that followed the confrontation with the Pallid Whale.
She was later revealed to have been swallowed by the Pallid Whale. Thus, Queequeg lived in Pequod Town with other ingested survivors until the events of Canto V.

**Canto V: The Evil Defining**

Queequeg's first meeting with the Sinners took place in Pequod Town, after Ishmael tried to attack the town's leader, Ahab. Ahab called her off and, during a brief meeting in her office, promised Ishmael an opportunity to kill her so long as the Sinners help the captain in reaching the Pallid Whale's heart. Queequeg was sent to follow the Sinners' path in traversing the Whale due to being the only person capable of steering the boat, where her history with Ishmael was shown further. Upon reaching the heart, Queequeg turned on the Sinners at Ahab's command due to the Pallidification preventing them from attacking the Whale themselves, and needing the Golden Bough within Dante's head to do so.
She would then be absorbed into Ahab's E.G.O to be used as ammunition, though Ishmael staved off Ahab long enough for Queequeg to return, allowing her to hold on just long enough to apologize for not being strong enough to think for herself, and asks Ishmael to say her name again before succumbing to the Pallidification and melting away. Her spirit appeared to help Ishmael in tearing out the Pallid Whale's heart before passing on.

### Trivia
Queequeg shares her namesake with the character from Herman Melville's Moby-Dick. Much like the Queequeg of *Limbus Company*, her literary counterpart is a heavily-tattooed harpooneer with whom Ishmael forms a special bond.
In the novel, Queequeg is the son of the King of the fictional island of Kokovoko in the South Pacific Ocean, and his tattoos are largely inspired by Māori tattoos. In particular, Melville was inspired, in his creation of Queequeg, by a depiction of Māori chief Te Pēhi Kupe.
The scene in which Ishmael is sent to bucket the oil from the inside of a Whale is directly inspired by chapter 72 of *Moby-Dick*. In it, Queequeg and Ishmael are tied together via a monkey-rope: Queequeg descends from the ship to skin a whale previously captured, while Ishmael must keep Queequeg safe and pull him up when he slips off the whale's carcass. Ishmael notes that with the two of them being "wedded" together by the rope, if Queequeg should fall, "both usage and honor demanded, that instead of cutting the cord, it should drag [Ishmael] down in his wake." The theme is vastly reprised in Queequeg's arc in *Limbus Company*, as she is forced to cut the "rope" connecting her to Ishmael in order to survive the Pallidification.
The rope of Queequeg's coffin, which Ishmael refashions as a headband, can be seen in nearly all of her Identities.

---

## Rain

### Appearance
Rain is a short man with black hair reaching his ears, with large orange-lens goggles resting over his bangs. He wears a black choker with a silver piece dangling at the center. He wears a large blue overcoat adorned with tools over his bare chest, with a similarly stocked toolbelt crooked over a pair of black swim trunks. He wears dirtied white sneakers on his feet. He is also shown to carry his weapon at times, a large sword with chainsaw-like teeth across its edge.

### Personality
Rain cares a lot about keeping up a good reputation for Molar Boatworks and will give unsubtle reminders to Olga to stay professional in front of their customers. While he might be strict, it is clear that it comes from a place of caring about Olga and Mika and a desire to keep working with them.

### Story
After the events of Library of Ruina* Rain and his fellow Molar Office Fixers, Olga and Mika, returned from their book forms and opened the Molar Boatworks workshop in the Backstreets of District 21. They are contracted by Limbus Company to modify Mephistopheles to be capable of nautical travel and while the Sinners spent days killing Trash Crabs to acquire the materials needed, Rain, Olga, and Mika complete the requested modifications. Despite some set backs with missing materials and forgetting to add the mode needed to keep Mephistopheles afloat, Rain and his friends soon saw LCB off on their journey across the Great Lake.

---

## Ran

### Appearance
Ran is a woman with brown skin, dark brown hair with dirty-blond highlights and crystal blue eyes. Her hair is shoulder length with messy bangs and a high ponytail tied with an orange-red hair tie. Ran sports a black tank top, reddish-orange workpants with black and white stripes and black waist tie, held up by thick suspender straps of similar color and silver buckles. She loosely wears a K-Corp issued lab coat on her arms, exposing her shoulders and collarbone. The lab coat is heavily dirtied and a large, crudely painted red 'X' is drawn over K Corp's logo, signifying her joining with the Technology Liberation Alliance. Ran is also seen wearing white slippers and white and reddish-orange lab goggles above her forehead.

### Personality
Ran is an intelligent, talkative woman who enjoys toying with others. She has a strong conviction in her anti-technology beliefs and was interested in science from a very young age, mentioning how she attended grad school thanks to winning an award on a paper she wrote about atoms, and speaks down to those who do not understand her perspective. Ran often encourages conversation between herself and the Sinners, despite being on opposing sides, as she feels that someone should do the talking. During these moments, Ran clearly enjoys the chances to express her opinions and toy with whoever she's speaking to.
