Shortly after, Moses bores a hole through Matthias's torso using her Crimson Point, and Vespa finishes him off by slicing through his head. The battle ends with Matthias dead, and with Kira apprehended.

### Trivia
Vespa and Crabro are both genera of wasp. Vespa is the genus of hornets, and Crabro is a genus of square-headed wasps.
Additionally, "Vespa crabro" is the binomial name of European hornets.
Though it could be a coincidence as yellow and black are colors often associated with bees and wasps, Vespa donning a yellow jacket during his time as an N Corp. Taboo Hunter can be a reference to the Yellow jacket, another species of wasp.
Vespa's Relic takes its name from Gungnir, the spear Odin uses in Norse mythology which has the ability to always hit its target.
According to Moses, Vespa's Distortion manifests as a pair of tattered wings of a bee.[4]
Vespa's hobbies are vehicle maintenance and forming his thoughts while brewing cinnamon tea.
This matches two of his likes, being cars and cinnamon; he also likes foodstuffs aswell as clothes well suited for agile activities.
Vespa dislikes cacti and Syndicates, especially the Thumb.
Ezra came up with the title of Yellow Harpoon as an option for Vespa's Color title, which ultimately was the one chosen by the Hana Association.

---

## Wang Dawei

### Appearance
Wang Dawei is a tall man with medium length, middle-parted brown hair beneath a short, black, hat. He wears a simply charcoal blue robe that reaches his ankles, buttoned over the right side of his chest. On his back, he carries a large hourglass shaped coffin, with two straps on its back allowing it to rest on his shoulders.

### Personality
Wang Dawei is coolheaded, choosing to slowly plan out his actions rather than charge into a battle without consideration. He believes himself to be intelligent, and is quick to mend any potential disadvantage he happens to brings himself, such as when he quickly segued a failed attempt to steal Jia Qiu's coins to stealing Jia Baoyu's instead.

### Story
Following the events of Intervallo V: Nocturnal Sweeping, Wang Dawei would, at some point, become acquainted with and revive Shi Yihua using newfound Wang Family Boluses.
During round one of the Family Hierarch Evaluation, Wang Dawei passed the first round by impressing the judges with his possible solution to immortality.
During the second round of the Family Hierarch Evaluation, he encountered Hong Lu and his entourage as they were meeting with Xue Baochai. Proclaiming his intention to swoop in and claim a success in the evaluation, he was allowed the chance to steal a portion of any one candidate's coins. While he initially spoke to steal Jia Qiu's coins, the host reminded him of the possible dangers of the target of the theft attacking him, to which he swiftly amended his target to be Hong Lu. Wang Dawei, having colluded with Shi Yihua for a new, unmarketed bolus made by the Wang Family, unleashed the revived Shi Family member from his coffin, acting as a surprise marketing reveal. Shi Yihua, failing to agree with his partner, chose to battle the Sinners out of personal spite and feelings of newfound power.
In the midst of the battle, stray pinions flew into and injured Wang Dawei. While his fate is unknown, Shi Yihua and Xue Baochai would continue battling until they were both eliminated, implying he was simply injured.

---

## Wang Qingshan

### Appearance
Wang Qingshan wears her deep blue hair in a bowlcut fashion, with straight bangs around the entire perimeter of her head. She wears a brown kasaya, with an orange robe overtop fastened by a large golden buckle. On her feet, she wears plain brown sandals. When encountered during Canto VIII, she is bloodied and in a kneeling position, her clothes partially torn. She carries a japamala in her right hand.

### Personality
Desperately hoping to prove herself to her family, Wang Qingshan is a devout woman hoping to win the role of Hierarch, bringing honor to her family if she succeeds. Despite the fact that she fled from past battles, she is willing to battle while injured, hoping to simply prove herself as worth her weight.

### Story
**Canto VIII: The Surrendered Witnessing**

Wang Qingshan participated in the Family Hierarch Evaluations. She succeeded in the first round, and was met in the second round, being first identified by Lin Daiyu. Here, she encountered Jia Qiu who bested her in combat, barely escaping his brutal attack. Begging Hong Lu for his coins, the rejection pushed her to fear for her life if she returned home a failure, leading her to attack Hong Lu and the Sinners with her remaining troops. Losing the short scuffle, she was shortly eliminated.

**Intervallo VI: Spring Cultivation**

Wang Qingshan was among the parties present during the hearing of Jia Xichun, held by Jia Yuanchun, who aimed to topple and belittle the newfound Hierarch.
Amidst the training of the new Hierarch, Wang Qingshan was one of the opponents of the Hierarch's training, serving as her third midterm. While she was greatly bothered by Jia Xichun, as well as annoyed by the use of her little brother in training, the two spar amicably. After the fact, while speaking to Jia Xichun, she is ultimately swayed to the side of the new Hierarch, now believing in the cause to make Hongyuan a safer place for the children.
During the end-of-training meeting, Wang Qingshan voted against the vote of no confidence held, allying herself with Jia Xichun.

### Trivia
Wang Qingshan's attire is the typical attire of a fully ordained Buddhist monk, featuring a layered set of kasaya robes, and completed with the japamala she carries.

---

## Wang Ren

### Appearance
Wang Ren is a man with straight bangs, a small piece on the left side fastened aside by two horizontal hairclips. He wears black-rimmed circular glasses, and a brown-gray robe with a plaid pattern across it and elbow-length sleeves. On his right wrist, he wears a black bracelet, and carries a thick brown book in his left hand. Beneath his robes, he wears brown pants and similarly colored loafers.

### Personality
Wang Ren is a spoiled man with little concern for others, looking to become the hierarch of Daguanyuan. He is shown to be meek, aiming to accomplish his goals without concern for the safety of others, such as endlessly offering blood to Bloodfiends in hope of achieving a faux immortality.

### Story
During the first round of the Family Hierarch Evaluations, Wang Ren would be the first to be called to demonstrate his answer to immortality. Mistakenly believing the Bloodbag he had acquired via Bloodfiend Hunters for an actual Bloodfiend, he presented the monster to the trio of judges, only to be told his answer was not sufficient. After a brief panic, attempting to explain how all one needs is blood to reach the immortality they crave, Don Quixote solemnly explains the downsides of life as a Bloodfiend. He is promptly dropped to his death, as the circular plate he and his Bloodbag stood upon is opened.

### Trivia
Wang Ren might be based on the character by the same name, Wang Ren (王仁, Pinyin: Wáng Rén*), from Cao Xueqin's novel *Dream of the Red Chamber*.

---

## Wang Zhao

### Appearance
Wang Zhao is a short man with cropped black hair, with his bangs shaped in cloud-like formations, sweeping to the left side of his face. He wears a small gilded crown, and has half-lidded eyes, with yellow irises and purple pupils. His hair extends behind his neck, connecting into a braid that rests across his collar. He wears a choker with a similar intricate design to his crown, and a cropped white jacket with a cloud pattern along the sleeves. Beneath this, he wears a gray top buttoned beneath a braided cross-pattern belt, which extends into a long tailcoat with the same cloud pattern as his top. His pants are white, becoming dark gray with a gradient, and he wears dark loafers on his feet. On the left side of his waist, he carries a white-and-gray sword with a gilded hilt, and carries an ornate pipe in his right hand, featuring a cloud of dark smoke emerging.

### Personality
Wang Zhao is a lax man without aspirations to acquire the title of Hongyuan hierarch, rather participating to find another candidate that is more deserving of the title, giving them his backing. He is a self-admitted introvert, preferring to remain in his quarters more commonly, contributing to his distance among even other Daguanyuan residents such as Hong Lu.

### Story
**Canto VIII: The Surrendered Witnessing**

Wang Zhao participated in the Family Hierarch Evaluations. In the first round, he witnessed Dante reviving Hong Lu after being split in half by Ryōshū. He succeeded in the first round, and was met face-to-face in the second round. At the beginning of the second round, he approached Hong Lu and his entourage, interested in a temporary travelling group to spectate the man. While the group was initially skeptical of the man's intent, he willingly clarified that he would only be following others to find a candidate he deemed worth supporting, having no interest in the role of hierarch himself. Sacrificing a coin of his, he accompanied the group to their agreeance. In the midst of their early travels, he questioned Hong Lu about the rumor of Jia Xichun having lost her Heishou Pack, mentioning he may give up another coin in favor of the information, though was disappointed when Hong Lu could not offer any answer. After a brief battle with Shi Huazhen, and examination of the old Kong Family laboratory, Wang Zhao deemed he had seen enough, and that Hong Lu is not who he plans to assist. Saying goodbye, he casually severed the agreeance on accompanying one another, and wandered off.
On his own, he would be willingly eliminated by giving his coins to Jia Qiu, who promised all that he wished for. While waiting for his elimation to be confirmed, Jia Huan came across him, shocked that he would give up that easily - especially for somebody like Jia Qiu. While Jia Huan considered brutalizing the man then and there, the nearby Heishou Pack members took Wang Zhao out of the competition.
Briefly during Jia Xichun's celebration ceremony, Wang Zhao met again with the Sinners. Rather than joining the celebrations, he simply alluded to the storm clouds gathering over Hongyuan, in reference to both the external and internal forces looking to topple the status quo of the new hierarch. Concluding his brief reappearance, he left after delivering the ambiguous message.

**Intervallo VI: Spring Cultivation**

Wang Zhao was among the parties present during the hearing of Jia Xichun, held by Jia Yuanchun, who aimed to topple and belittle the newfound Hierarch.
Amidst the training of the new Hierarch, Wang Zhao visited during his cousin's preparation, Wang Qingshan, who served as her third midterm. Wang Zhao briefly speaks with Jia Xichun, mentioning the dangers of the unfolding situation, before leaving Xichun alone with her sparring partner.
During the end-of-training meeting, Wang Zhao voted against the vote of no confidence held, allying himself with Jia Xichun.

---

## Wei

### Appearance
Wei is a man with shoulder-length dark hair, parted down the center of his face, showing his face. He wears oval glasses, and a dark hanfu lined with golden trim, which is tied at the waist with a red sash and tied knot. On his shoulders, he wears a red cloak with a dark trim, with golden ornamentation lining this trim and his right shoulder. His hanfu ends at his ankles, with similar gold ornamenting being displayed on the right half. He wears dark loafers with golden soles over his feet, with white socks beneath.
When the Wu Heishou Pack Bolus' effects activate, his lower body becomes that of a horse and he grows the ears of one, with armored legs and a long dark coat running down its sides. He wields a large, dark guandao as a weapon. In this state, his eyes glow white.

### Personality
Wei is a quiet and kind man, taking the time to respect Hong Lu despite the former's generally negative status within the family he works for, wishing the man well regardless. He is highly responsible, assigned to escorting Jia Xichun along the battle against La Manchaland, chosen for his formidable abilities in combat, as displayed by when he singlehandedly defeats waves of Bloodfiends. Despite this, he considers himself lesser in the scheme of things for unknown reasons.
During Intervallo VI: Spring Cultivation, a glimpse at a more enthusiastic and excitable side of him is seen after he won a round of mahjong against Rodion, exclaiming his victory. His strength is also seen while Jia Xichun was in danger, blindly attacking anyone that tried to get to his master, including other allies such as the Sinners.

### Story
**Prior to Limbus Company***

Wei was once an Adept of the Wu Branch of the Heishou Pack, which served Jia Xichun. He was eventually liberated of his status as a Heishou and became Jia Xichun's personal servant, at the cost of the latter's control over the branch.

**Canto VII: The Dream Ending**

Wei was first met alongside Jia Xichun, who talked to the Sinners in the Backstreets of P Corp. He approached Hong Lu and briefly caught up with the Sinner, honoring the man as if he were still in service to him. He then quietly followed alongside Xichun as she leads her men to the briefing for their job.
He was later met again in Area 2 of La Manchaland, having participated in the eradication of The Priest's men, as well as the search for the area's button. Meeting the Sinners at the confessional, he deflected one of Sansón's attacks aimed at Xichun after she attempted to kill The Priest. As an onslaught of Bloodbags and Bloodfiends approached following another play of Sansón's, Wei defeated the horde on his own, looking to protect his men who were knocked unconscious by the magician, as well as keep the path clear for his young master. He reluctantly recommended she accompany Hong Lu and the Sinners in Area 3 due to the greater odds of surviving if she did.

**Intervallo V: Nocturnal Sweeping**

Wei once again accompanied Jia Xichun for the entirety of her appearance in the Intervallo, though his role was otherwise limited. His previous status as a member of the Heishou Pack would be briefly mentioned in this Intervallo. While he made an attempt to defend Jia Xichun against Jia Qiu's libel, she told him to stand down.

**Canto VIII: The Surrendered Witnessing**

Wei accompanied his master on the travelling to Daguanyuan, as well as through the first two rounds of the Family Hierarch Evaluations. Prior to the events of the second round, he attempted to convince Jia Xichun a total of three times to not visit his residence, though ultimately gave up. He wished the Sinners well, and hoped they would not meet in the next round.
In the midst of the Family Hierarch Evaluation's second round, Jia Xichun encountered both Jia Qiu and Jia Huan; the former simply ignoring her and the latter viciously attacking her faction. By the end of the confrontation, all that remained of Jia Xichun's faction was herself and Wei who were grievously injured.
During the celebration of the Jia Xichun's newfound role as H Corp. Hierarch, Wei attempted to mitigate her bafflement. He joined his master as she traveled to the Tiekan Temple, where she would meet with the elders and have her role pronounced and later officialized as she takes the throne in Daguanyuan.
Though she had protection, the many factions looking to topple H Corp. managed to catch up to Xichun's faction, including the Thumb's Capo IIII, Lei Heng. In a one-sided confrontation, Lei Heng massacred the majority of the group on the bridge leading to the temple, leaving solely Wei alive. The Sinners, arriving after the carnage, are given the ultimatum; if Zilu were to take a single hit from the Capo, they could ensure Wei survives. Though Hong Lu and the Sinners felt little for Wei due to not knowing him particularly well, Hong Lu wishes for Xichun's earnest happiness to return, something Wei's survival would help. Agreeing to the conditions, Zilu took a near-deadly blow from Lei Heng, who kicked Wei over to the group afterwards, living up to his word. Despite surrendering the man, he assumed he may not even survive the day, and that if he did, he would need two to three months of healing to be back to his previous level.
Wei would be reunited with his master after his narrow survival, after she had successfully inherited the role of hierarch for the District. He joined her and the Sinners in celebration, where he lamented on the new difficulty of organizing the information that was once stored only via the Xianhuang Anamnaworm inherited between elders. The servant and his master appear to discuss this matter alongside Meursault, seen during the CG accompanying the Canto's credits.

**Intervallo VI: Spring Cultivation**

Wei accompanied his master during her initial meeting as the newfound Hierarch of Hongyuan, where she is humiliated and belittled by Jia Yuanchun, much to their dismay. However, after Zigong and Sinclair successfully argue a case in favor of the Hierarch, she is given a month-long period of training to prove herself. Wei was among the faction that will assist with this process, most notably being one of the members required to upkeep paperwork and documents, alongside Zigong. While he is not physically present for much of the month, he sends his master a message of encouragement. Despite his growing insomnia and delirium, he continued to push through seemingly never-ending paperwork.
Following her fourth midterm and encounter with the maddening Xue Pan, Xichun is sent into a spiralling bad mood, worrying if her efforts will be for naught given the current state of things and the opinions of her. In hopes of cheering her up, Wei mentions an old pond within H Corp. that became spoiled from the dumping of rotted corpses. Confused, Xichun questions why he discussed the decommissioned pond, to which he explained that it has since been purified by a tall tree growing from the nutrients, cleaning the water and allowing wildlife to rehabilitate. Wei asks if she'd enjoy visiting it alongside him, leading the two—joined by Sinclair and Dante—to visit the pond, where Xichun's mood greatly improves.
Upon hearing the news of Xichun's kidnapping by a trapped palanquin, Wei was sent into a panic, racing off into the distance to find and save her. While this happens, possibly as a byproduct of his stress and busy schedule, he began to mutate back to his Heishou Pack self, becoming centaur-like in his frenzied state. At the site, he failed to find Xichun, senselessly slaughtering Si branch members while his master battled the Night Drifter. In his haze, the Sinners approach, causing his ire to turn towards them. After a brutal battle, the mutations are suppressed, though Wei is unable to continue on with the group, his previous wound from Lei Heng reopening and incapacitating him.
During the end-of-training meeting, Wei was present alongside the factions allied with Jia Xichun. With her role effectively secured, he was able to accompany Xichun as she was given her earned respect.

---

## Wolf

### Appearance
Wolf is a short woman with long and spiky blue hair, traveling down to her shoulders. Her bangs are brought down over her right eye, concealing it, while the left side of her head is shorter, gray, hair, which reveals her other eye. She wears a fur-lined black coat that goes down to her knees, with a buckle midway down her torso. On her left arm, there is a wrapped purple snake emblem. She has two gloved hands, and wears torn black pants and similarly dark shoes. She carries a large silver sword which has a pommel that sports a large tuft of blue hair, similar in color to her hair color.

### Personality
Wolf is a focused individual who values the lessons she learned from her mentor and does not like to waste time. She is less emotive than her partners, overall allowing them to speak and demonstrate their abilities.

### Story
Wolf, Lion, and Panther are met just as they corner Dante in a dark forest as a part of a plan made by their master. They decided to kill them once they realize that, thanks to Dante's new head, they will be unable to get any information out of them. While Lion wanted to draw it out, both Wolf and Panther agree it would be best to kill them quickly. Just as Wolf was about to kill Dante, they heard a noise, realizing there is a bus heading towards them. The Sinners exited the bus and engage the three in a fight, but Wolf and her companions made short work of them and are only stopped when Vergilius dismembers Wolf, taking a leg, and Lion, removing an arm, before he orders Panther to drag them away in a retreat.

### Trivia
Panther, Lion and Wolf are based on the three beasts from the first Canto of Dante's Inferno, which symbolize the three major divisions of the sins punished in hell. The she-wolf, the last beast encountered by Dante, is believed to represent the sins of incontinence, lack of self-restraint, and the deadly sin of greed, making the beast a representation of the sins of the city of Florence. As these sins are considered by Dante to be at the root of all political unrest in the land, the she-wolf is considered the most dangerous of the three beasts.
Though their master is currently unknown, Vergilius referring to them as "the Serpent", as well as the presence of purple snake ornaments on all three group members, it is possible the identity of the master is none other than Iori, the Purple Tear.

---

## Xianren

### Overview
The venerated elders of Hongyuan, each Xianren was once a well-known Hierarch of the District. In the process of succession, each retiring elder passes the inherited Xianhuang Anamnaworm to the next elder, before being sealed within Tiekan Temple alongside the rest of the group, where they live with their own, unique, forms of immortality. This allows all Executive Directors to supervise the Wing even long after their supposed deaths, but deteriorates their sanity entirely as a side effect of inheriting the Anamnaworm and no longer being able to physically interact with the outside world.
Located deep within Daguanyuan, the passageways to Tiekan Temple are winding and exceptionally exhausting, with few members even knowing of the path to it. At the gates of the temple underground, just beyond a decorated bridge over a small lake, is a massive jade slot in the center, a gateway only opened either when the Xianren themselves invite somebody, or by Hong Lu bringing his eye to the doorway.
The room is dark, with many ornate pillars and seatings around the center of the room, where a giant screen rests on the ground, giving a live feed of all that Hong Lu witnesses via his left eye. After the events of Canto VIII: The Surrendered Witnessing, the room becomes flooded and blue, disconnected from the outside world due to the flooding.
Each elder features a complete unique design from one another, embodying their use of different methods of immortality. In all cases, this involves them becoming grotesquely deformed and their minds warped into madness.

### Members
Three Xianren (Elder in a Jar, Elder in Monk Robes, and Elder in a Machine) were named in The Lord of Hongyuan Hong Lu's Uptie Story. As the other Xianren do not feature unique names in-game or in files, they are given names which are unofficial designations used for the sake of simplicity.*

**Elder on a Branch**

**Gender:** Male
**Status:** Alive
**First Appearance:** Canto VIII: The Surrendered Witnessing
One of the many Xianren, this elder is a figure composed of congealed blood, sitting on a small branch with his legs in a lotus position with his wrists crossed. His face features a coronal slice of a brain, with the skull similarly exposed with beady eyes and a large set of symmetrical antlers emerging from the sides of his head. Several budding branches emerge from his back, and stretch outwards behind him.

**Elder on a Wheelchair**

**Gender:** Female
**Status:** Alive
**First Appearance:** Canto VIII: The Surrendered Witnessing
One of the many Xianren, this elder is a dark figure with wrinkled skin, appearing as if she has been completely drained of blood and an oxygen mask over her mouth. She has an elongated skull, sunken eyes, and long, claw-like fingers. Her bottom half is obscured in a bloodied robe, and she sits in a rusty wheelchair, featuring an attachment that carries twelve bags of blood, all of which are attached to various points across her body.

**Elder in a Machine**

**Gender:** Male
**Status:** Alive
**First Appearance:** Canto VIII: The Surrendered Witnessing
One of the many Xianren, this elder is only a torso and head, with just the right arm remaining. His skin is aged and patchy, while the mechanical prosthetics replace the missing sections. His brain and left eye are exposed, with a large red dot where his mouth would be, the rest of his head replaced by the sleek metal. Large tubes connect to his back, holding him upright, with his spine connecting to a glowing red platform beneath him. He is mentioned to be an elder of the Xue family.

**Elder in Monk Robes**

**Gender:** Female
**Status:** Alive
**First Appearance:** Canto VIII: The Surrendered Witnessing
One of the many Xianren, this elder appears to have rotted flesh peeling back, revealing her teeth as her lips decay and an exposed brain. From her body, several branches sprout, such as from her right eye socket. She wears long, aged, white robes with three large circular pattern on its center and sides. She carries a tall branch that has similarly circular supports in the center of it.

**Elder in a Jar**

**Gender:** Male
**Status:** Alive
**First Appearance:** Canto VIII: The Surrendered Witnessing
One of the many Xianren, this elder appears to simply be the overgrown head of an elderly man, with bushy eyebrows and moustache. He is within a tube full of red fluid, with many smaller tubes connecting to the top and bottom. Some tubes connect to his head, such as on his cheeks. He is the grandfather of Hong Lu.

**Elder in Trimmed Robes**

**Gender:** Male
**Status:** Alive
**First Appearance:** Canto VIII: The Surrendered Witnessing
One of the many Xianren, this elder looks like an overgrown slug, with vestigial limbs hanging limply on top of his huge body. He has green skin, which sags overtop the majority of his face. He wears a large dual set of brown robes with tan trims.
During the events of Canto VIII: The Surrendered Witnessing, Jia Mu is on the verge of assuming a role as one of the Xianren due to Jia Xichun's rise to Hierarch. While her specific form of immortality is left unclear, Jia Mu takes a vested interest in the Hiexian Bolus, a forbidden Bolus featuring traits of every Heishou Pack Branch, as well as the Golden Bough, becoming interested (albeit misunderstanding how it works) in Dante's head and its connection to the Golden Boughs.
**For more information, see Jia Mu.
Multiple Elder Trees appear in the midst of Jia Mu's battle with the Sinners; these appear to be elders transformed into woody roots and trees with sunken faces visible at the top of them.
For more information, see Elder Trees.
Several elders are visible in the Tiekan Temple Story Background, both those that speak and those that do not. Those that do not speak include (from left to right):
A humanoid figure with arms crossed over its chest;
A large mass with several eyes and veins on its side;
A large figure with long arms and a serene expression, resting on a small armrest;
A masked figure with a bloated stomach and long neck;
A hanging skeletal figure with large attachments on its back;
A wireframe holding up the torn skin of a person, a small set of red eyes visible at its top;
An elderly looking skeletal figure with a bloated head;
A cloaked figure with visible teeth and eyes beneath its robe, with two long limbs hanging downwards;
A mass of flesh that appears to be melting, with several lime-green sequences of tubing attached to various parts of its body;
An innumerable amount of skeletal bodies sitting in a lotus position.

### Story
**Prior to *Limbus Company***

The first elder of Daguanyuan became an Anamnaworm, one which would be passed down across each following Hierarch in a mean to accrue exponential knowledge across each succeeding Hierarch. One of these elders was recognized by Jia Xichun as her great-great-grandfather, who snuck her snacks and was known for his fondness for walks.
As the Xianren's lifespans were so long, they found that the true danger of immortality was boredom. As a way to combat this, on Jia Baoyu's birth, Jia Mu implanted a jade into his left eye, making him a treasured piece of Hongyuan's culture. In reality, this jade allowed for everything that Jia Baoyu experienced to be sent to a screen in the Tiekan Temple, to provide the Xianren with unique entertainment from within their chambers.
In Jia Baoyu's youth, he would be repeatedly summoned to the Tiekan Temple, where they would meet with him as a way to treasure him for his status as the "jade of Hongyuan", something which Jia Baoyu feared at first, yet grew apathetic and desensitized to. On some occasions, Jia Baoyu witnessed a 'molting' process, where the elders fed on unknowing servants, splitting their corpses between each member as means to remain living.
One event of which the Xianren were particularly fond of was the massacre of the Kong family, to which they grew especially fond of Jia Mu for having caused.
In a bid to continue creating new entertainment for the elders, Jia Mu had Jia Baoyu leave Daguanyuan, coinciding with when the man was contracted by Faust for Limbus Company. This would cause the Xianren to witness the events of every single Canto, growing fond of the Sinners from a detached point of interest.

**Canto VIII: The Surrendered Witnessing**

Once Jia Xichun had managed to secure the role of H Corp. Hierarch, she was required to be annointed officially by meeting with the Xianren in Tiekan Temple, accepting the Anamnaworm, and then assuming the throne in Daguanyuan. The Sinners arrived to the temple while this was in the process of unfolding, where Jia Xichun grew terrified of the Anamnaworm, worried to become another immortality-obsessed Xianren who witnesses brutality through Hong Lu's jade. While the Xianren were initially joyful at meeting the Sinners in the flesh, they quickly grew annoyed at the insubordination against the passage of the Anamnaworm. Jia Mu battled the Sinners, utilizing the forbidden Heixian Bolus to inherit the attributes of every Heishou Pack Branch. During this battle, she consumed several of the elders in a desperate plea to regain her footing against the Sinners, and harness the consumed elder's immortality.
At the climax of this battle, Hong Lu utilizes an empowered Land of Illusion to release a flood of clear water, knocking the Golden Bough embedded into Jia Mu's chest free and flooding the entire temple. As the Xianren are collectively knocked away from their seats, Jia Huan angrily approached the screen in the center of the building and shattered it. While several of the elders attempted to crawl out of the gateway of the temple, they were unable to, and were sealed within as Hong Lu wished them goodbye, permanently sealing them inside.
While the Xianren each utilize means of flawed immortality, only their natural lifespans are extended, and their biological processes are not stopped. Without their sustenance, influence, or entertainment, Meursault hypothesizes they will very slowly pass away while locked within the chamber.

### Trivia
In Taoist culture, Xian is a term used to classify any form of mythological creature that has achieved immortality. Expanding on this, the specific term of Xianren means "immortal person."
Several times, the Xianren are alternatively referred to as the Enlightened Ones in Canto VIII.
While Taoist Xian are generally depicted as benevolent and wise men unconcerned by worldly ideas, the Xianren in *Limbus Company* represent the opposite of this idea.
After Hong Lu's final attack against Jia Mu, the seating of the temple seen in the Story Background is visibly cleared of every Xianren.
Lady Wang mentions that Hong Lu's birthname, Jia Baoyu, was bestowed upon him by the Xianren.

## Xiren

### Appearance
Xiren is a woman with brown hair, with bangs parted down the center and hair tied into two small buns on the back of her head. She wears a gray hanfu with white sleeves, and dark red accents along the hems and center, beneath a similarly red sash. While her left arm is typical, her right arm has a green, plant-like, appearance, and her feet have been reshaped into hooves.
Notably, her younger self features none of these deformities, which were later caused due to extensive use of Boluses.

### Personality
Hong Lu's trusted maidservant and caretaker through his childhood, Xiren always had a calm and collected personality, being always mindful of her young master's feelings. Xiren cared deeply for Hong Lu, and always attempted to shield him as best as she could from the cruel realities of Daguanyuan. Growing up, Hong Lu admired Xiren for her intelligence, as she seemed to always have an answer to everything; Jia Mu similarly comments on it after Xiren's attempt to discuss what she had been doing to her grandchild. Jia Mu also points out her naivety for not knowing her place, and believing she would be able to protect Hong Lu.
Following this act of insubordination, Xiren was executed by the Heishou Packs, and revived through Life Insurance technology. As Jia Baoyu's closest servant, no expense was saved for her, and she received the most expensive service available, which retained all of her memories, although her personality slowly changed, becoming colder and unaffected. This is later revealed to have been a conscious decision on Jia Mu's part, who revived her specifically as a more obedient, unfeeling servant, who would simply fulfill her duties and encourage Jia Baoyu to comply to Jia Mu and the Xianren's wishes.
Despite this, by the time of his return to Daguanyuan, Hong Lu views her as the same as she has always been, simply hoping her memories still bring her warmth. Before his departure, he asks her what she thinks of his decision to continue his journey, to which Xiren advises him to walk the path of his own choosing, which brings a smile to Hong Lu's face.

### Story
**Prior to Limbus Company***

Xiren raised Jia Baoyu as his primary maidservant, taking care of him during his daily life. Xiren was by Baoyu's side during the times after the disappearance of Jia Ling, and attempted to shield him from the truth of what had happened to him, claiming that Jia Ling would be back after 100 nights.
During her time in his service, Xiren died multiple times; by making extensive use of Life Insurance, she was successfully revived with her memories intact. However, her personality slowly eroded, becoming emotionless as a result. When asked about Jia Ling again years later, she explained the matter, suggesting for Jia Baoyu to give up his naive hopes on the return of Jia Ling, as the poison affecting his absent sibling had caused brain death—something that neither Life Insurance nor Boluses could ever heal. As Jia Ling's maidservants gossiped of their master's inevitable point of no return, Jia Baoyu would reluctantly accept this reality and praise Xiren for her intelligence.

**Canto VIII: The Surrendered Witnessing**

Upon the return of Hong Lu and Jia Xichun to Daguanyuan, Xiren returned to her master's side outside his childhood residency. After a brief reunion between Xiren and her master, she guided the Sinners to Hong Lu's room, where they were to pass the night.
Following the first round of the Family Hierarchal Evaluation, Hong Lu and the Sinners returned to his residency, where Xiren awaited them, having been delivered a letter for her master. Despite Ishmael realizing the letter had been tampered with, Xiren was resolute on only having only the responsibility to deliver the letter, rather than also keeping it from being handled by outside factions. Baoyu accepted this as if it was completely normal, explaining Xiren's situation to the rest of the Sinners when asked why he did so.
After Hong Lu had wrapped up his business in District 8, with Jia Xichun now hierarch, he had a final cup of tea alongside Xiren. Finally asking her how she feels of his departure, she gives an empty response. While Dante thinks the response is underwhelming, Hong Lu is comforted by this and smiled earnestly.

### Trivia
Xiren is based on the character Hua Xiren (花袭人，Pinyin: *Huā Xírén*), from Cao Xueqin's novel *Dream of the Red Chamber*.
In *Dream of the Red Chamber*, Hua Xiren is the chief maid of Jia Baoyu, and he and her other masters are quite fond of her due to her thoughtfulness and diligence in her work.

---

## Xue Baochai

### Appearance
Xue Baochai is a woman of pale complexion, with droopy orange eyes and long, curly brown hair that reaches to her lower back. Her hair is partially worn in princess curls, tied up with orange flower ribbons, and she has blunt bangs. Baochai dons a qixiong ruqun, a high-waisted hanfu, composed of a pink top with orange detailing, and a skirt in peach tones, all sporting colorful flower decorations.
Around her neck, Baochai wears a jade pendant, that she began wearing after her betrothed Jia Baoyu's departure from Hongyuan, as a way to remember him.

### Personality
Xue Baochai is an outgoing woman with a lively temperament. Used to the brutality of Daguanyuan, she always appears unbothered by the violence of the Family Hierarch war or the common practice of decapitation even among family members. Baochai has a vested interest in the dark and macabre, and one of her pastimes being curating collections of creepy urban legends and adventure stories.
During her first meeting with the Sinners, she immediately strikes up conversation and appears very interested in the tales of their adventures, particularly those of bloodshed, showing herself as amiable and friendly. Similarly, she converses with Jia Xichun and compliments her bravery, although her expressions of sorrow to Xichun's troubles come out as slightly back-handed. Baochai also shows herself completely unbothered at the possibility of her brother, Xue Pan, being killed by their mother as punishment, instead commenting that she hopes his personality will be edited to be more obedient and cause less trouble this time around. This lack of empathy on her part appears to stem from her exposure to the cruelty of Daguanyuan.
Baochai cares deeply for Hong Lu, and has long looked forward to his return to Hongyuan, upon which they will be married. While she used to think him a brooding man, Baochai reconsidered her first impression after an encounter in which Hong Lu comforted her, and she became enamored with his gentle and thoughtful demeanor. After their engagement was made official, Baochai began preparing his chambers, and she would often speak to him of the happy and luxurious life they would have together. Her infatuation for Hong Lu is shown to revolve less around Hong Lu as a person, but more around his role and his importance as the jewel of Hongyuan; her fixation on him often has her focus on the brilliance of his jade and the light he radiates, making her feelings closer to objectification than a genuine romantic interest.
Baochai is typically shown to be confident and place a great importance on her appearance, as she always had a fondness for expensive perfumes and fragrances, upkeeping her scent on the daily through a rigorous routine. Despite this, she seems to grow self-conscious at the possibility of Hong Lu not reciprocating her feelings, and to nurse a slight jealousy upon seeing him interact with Lin Daiyu.
Despite this, Baochai eventually lets go of this feeling, only requesting Daiyu to keep Hong Lu safe after they're forced to separate during the second round of the Family Hierarch Evaluations. By the end of the Canto, Baochai seems to have accepted that Hong Lu will not return to Daguanyuan to marry her, but despite this she stills wishes to care for him, defying her family's orders and risking her life to protect him and his sister.
Baochai's personality grows more somber after losing the attention of Hong Lu, now wishing the man and his siblings chose to simply ignore the happenings of Daguanyuan, wishing to live in naïve peace. While she has been taken fully into the schemes of those on the board of the District, she still expresses her own wish to return to the days of loving Hong Lu, going as far as revealing a scheme to harm Xichun moments before it finishes as a way of "following her heart".
After the short meeting with her former fiancé during the events of Intervallo VI, Baochai becomes continually more morose, now lamenting over her lack of fragrance and fully giving in to the controlling relationship bestowed upon her by Jia Yuanchun. With no family to support her, and her fiancé lost, she only sees a path forward with the other woman, who acts as her sole guiding light.

### Story
**Prior to Limbus Company***

Sometime in the past, Xue Baochai was put into an arranged marriage with Jia Baoyu, as of an agreement between Jia Mu and Baochai's mother.
One of the two's first meetings happened when Baoyu ran into Baochai grieving the loss of her pet bird, which had escaped from its cage; Baoyu comforted her, proposing that it would return to follow the scent of the blossoms in the coming year. On another occasion, Baoyu commented on Baochai's fragrance on a day where she hadn't the time to use her perfumes, stating that he quite enjoyed it. This stuck with Baochai until her adulthood, frequently citing it as one of the reasons of her love for Baoyu.

**Canto VIII: The Surrendered Witnessing**

Upon the return of Hong Lu to Daguanyuan, Xue Baochai quickly arrived to meet with her betrothed. Catching up with her absent fiancé, she drew his attention to the creation of her necklace, inspired by his jade eye. She was an exceptionally friendly face for the Sinners to encounter, and expressed curiosity over the tales of Hong Lu's adventure, particularly the bloody parts. After briefly discussing the situation regarding Jia Xichun, she checked with Hong Lu if he had encountered Jia Qiu during his travels, reaffirming the one-sided allyship he had held with Shi Yihua. Reminding Hong Lu she would always reside at Hongyuan, she departed from the dining hall.
Xue Baochai would participate in the Family Hierarch Evaluations, where she passed the first round—having been one of the many candidates shocked by Hong Lu's participation—and progressed towards the second round. She also made sure to congratulate Hong Lu for passing.
During the second round, she traveled with her clan only to stumble upon the Sinners; her bodyguard Lin Daiyu having traveled with the group due to getting lost. The group was soon forced into combat against a revived Shi Yihua, alongside the candidate Wang Dawei. Baochai, in an act of hoping to save Hong Lu and allow him to continue through the round, told him to leave as she would handle the enemy candidates. While her bodyguard accompanied her betrothed, her faction battled their foes until their collective eliminations, trapped by the closing walls nearby.
During the ceremony for Jia Xichun becoming hierarch, Baochai sheepishly approached the Sinners, skirting around a topic as she attempted to speak with them. Hurriedly, as Jia Qiu and his faction arrive, she explained the possible coup forming in the power vacuum before Xichun takes the throne. Her mother, the Shi and Xue families—led by Jia Yuanchun—all internally looked to overthrow the ceremony; this was still not accounting for outside factions looking to enter the Wing. Fearing her mother would find out if she delayed any longer, she shortly departed.
Following the events of Canto VIII, Baochai was abducted by Yuanchun, who threatened her with the exposure of her insubordination to her mother. Xue Baochai, fearfully, accepted to comply by Yuanchun's demands.

**Intervallo VI: Spring Cultivation**

After the events of the Family Hierarch Evaluation and Jia Xichun's ascension as new Executive Director of H Corp., the Xue family members that had conspired against the Hierarch were arrested, which left Baochai as current head of the family during council meetings. Baochai remained aligned with Jia Yuanchun during this period, planning to vote for the vote of no confidence towards Xichun. Furthermore, her engagement to Hong Lu, which had been arranged by her mother and the late Jia Mu, was broken off.
During Xichun's thirty days of training, Baochai visited the lecture hall to meet with Hong Lu. Baochai was dismissive of Xichun and the group's efforts, asking Hong Lu when they would give up on their attempts to change things. Hong Lu bluntly demanded Baochai to stop this behavior, although Baochai only stepped back after he commented on her having no fragrance, thus dispelling any illusion she still had of his attraction to her.
At the end of the month, after Jia Yuanchun is expelled from the council by Jia Xichun, Baochai follows Yuanchun, as the latter comments that she will depart to Q Corp., and that Baochai will follow her, for Yuanchun is the only light left for her.

### Trivia
Xue Baochai takes her name from the eponymous character, Xue Baochai (薛寶釵; 薛宝钗，Pinyin: *Xuē Bǎochāi*), from Cao Xueqin's novel *Dream of the Red Chamber*.
In *Dream of the Red Chamber*, Xue Baochai is Jia Baoyu's maternal cousin, and is described as a beautiful and tactful woman, well-liked by all the servants of the house, and whose qualities compliment Lin Daiyu's. Through the course of the novel, Xue Baochai weds Jia Baoyu, although their matrimony is an unhappy one, as Jia Baoyu's affections still lay with the late Lin Daiyu.
Xue Baochai's jade locket is based on the locket worn by her literary counterpart. In *Dream of the Red Chamber*, Baochai always wears a golden locket that was given to her by a monk, which contains an inscription that matches Jia Baoyu's, who similarly always wears the jade he was born with around his neck.

---

## Xue Pan

### Appearance
Xue Pan is a tall man with notably gray skin and piercing amber eyes. He has shaggy brown hair, which is longer on the back of his head, fashioned into long braids that coil across his entire body, with several orange bows tied across its length. He dons a miniature wuliu mian atop his head, with two sets of tassels on each side. He wears an amber robe, with wide sleeves revealing an inner lining of orange. Beneath a yellow sash at his waist, his clothes are covered in assorted talismans, similarly visible on the Jar Monsters he commands. He wears a set of loafers and wrappings on his legs.
As a child, he was still taller than the average youth. He wore similar clothing of a brown-orange robe, though his hair was much shorter, he did not wear a wuliu mian, and he did not wear the several talismans across his body.

### Personality
Visibly unwell, Xue Pan is a deranged man who cares little for the wellbeing of others. He is willing to put others at risk for his own enjoyment, choosing to allow his Jar Monsters to attack other Family Hierarch Evaluations candidates, believing it to be something treasured and worth sharing, in a macabre sense. He is outwardly spiteful as well, threatening Hong Lu in the moments before round two.
Xue Pan is shown to have been much more meek in his youth, worrying about the dangers of Daguanyuan's practices and wishing to not participate.

### Story
**Prior to Limbus Company***

As a child, Xue Pan feared the practices of Daguanyuan, once begging Jia Baoyu to save him from having to participate. Much to his chagrin, Jia Baoyu chose to not do anything that would save him from participating, creating a lifelong sense of distaste for Jia Baoyu.
Xue Pan was killed on several occasions in his life, causing gradual changes of his personality throughout his life. Xue Baochai alludes that this has always been an unsuccessful attempt to tame him.

**Canto VIII: The Surrendered Witnessing**

Xue Pan was the 27th candidate of the first round of the Family Hierarch Evaluations. When called upon by Jia Zheng, he approached the podium rather than the designated platform area the candidates typically stood upon. Despite being told to move to the platform, he'd remain at the podium and place a talisman-covered jar down, from which Jar Monsters emerged. As the creatures began to attack the audience, slaughtering potential candidates, Xue Pan reveled in the chaos. Following a short battle with the Sinners, the creatures returned to their jars, to which Xue Pan requested the verdict for his solution to immortality from the judges in exchange for the clay from the jars. In response, he passed the first round.
As Hong Lu and the Sinners rode the elevator to the grounds the second round of the Family Hierarch Evaluations were to take place on, Xue Pan shouted a threat towards Hong Lu, determined to behead the Sinner.
During round two of the Family Hierarch Evaluations, Xue Pan inevitably encountered Hong Lu, motivated by his past spite towards the man over never being able to afford the same favor the gem of the Jia Family was awarded. Despite his hatred for the man, Hong Lu mentioned that, if possible, he would have given the favor to Xue Pan, only furthering his rage. Commanding Lin Daiyu to assist him taking down Hong Lu, he was ignored by her, leading to annoyance over her insubordination. Xue Pan attacked the Sinners alongside his Jar Monsters, only to be defeated shortly. Unwilling to allow this, he made a final attempt to stand up to his enemies, only to be cut short as he is killed and eliminated from the Family Hierarch war.
His death would be taken lightly by Xue Baochai, who knew he would just later be revived again.

**Intervallo VI: Spring Cultivation**

Following the recent revival, Xue Pan was busy healing as the events of the Intervallo began. Because of this, he was not present at Jia Xichun's inundation, held by Jia Yuanchun, who aimed to topple and belittle the newfound Hierarch. However, he heard of the information and participated in the Hierarch's training.
Amidst the training of the new Hierarch, Xue Pan was one of the opponents of the Hierarch's training, serving as her fourth midterm. Annoyed by what he viewed as Jia Xichun's arrogance, he proclaimed his interest in the chaotic happenings of everything going wrong. After an attempt to convince the new Hierarch to kill him and use him as an example against all future terrors of Hongyuan, Jia Xichun remains steadfast on her peaceful choices, reminding Xue Pan of his younger self who hated this violence.
Despite his disagreement with Xichun's viewpoint, Xue Pan ultimately finds himself interested in the chaos and happenings that will follow in Xichun's wake. Despite failing to attend the end-of-training meeting, Xue Pan left a letter that voted against the vote of no confidence held, allying himself with Jia Xichun.

### Trivia
Xue Pan is based on the character by the same name, Xue Pan (薛蟠，Pinyin: *Xūe Pán*), from Cao Xueqin's novel *Dream of the Red Chamber*.
In *Dream of the Red Chamber*, Xue Pan is Xue Baochai's older brother known for his bullying and tactlessness. He is driven to murder a man over a servant-girl only to cover up the murder through his wealth, showing a dangerous personality akin to his *Limbus Company* counterpart.
Xue Pan has been revived a number of times via Life Insurance. While he initially recalls it as three or four times, he ultimately states that he no longer remembers.

---

## Yuri

### Appearance
Yuri looks to be a young woman of average height. She has straight, relatively long reddish-pink hair which falls down naturally over her shoulders with the exception of a few strands tied back with a bow. Her eyes are small and gray, topped with eyebrows a bit thicker than most of the other girls. Notably, she wears a cloth eye patch over her right eye and a small bandaid on her left side of her chin.
She wears the uniform of the unspecified Fixer office Aya and Hopkins also work for. However, while their version of the uniform has blue as its primary color, Yuri's has a reddish-pink similar to the color of her hair. The uniform consists of a long-sleeved white, black, and reddish-pink shirt with a turtleneck, overlaid with a loose fitting jacket and a backpack. They wear baggy pants tucked into black work boots. There are twin strings of cloth hanging from the bottom of the jacket and pants, and a blue belt attached to the pant thigh. Yuri also carries around some kind of long, glowing red sword.

### Personality
Yuri is rather normal in comparison to the eccentric sinners. While she opens up to the group over the course of the chapter, she starts off considerably mild. Yuri expresses kindness and consideration, and although she is used enough to the violence of the City to have no reaction upon witnessing Mephistopheles' source of fuel, she is distressed by Aya's death to the point of Outis expressing her disapproval. It's clear that Yuri carries a form of unresolved trauma which continues to weigh on her and sometimes result in weak-heartedness. Dante even points out that she is always slouching, describing it as if "it was her sole surviving obligation to fulfill the wills of her late colleagues." She also has a bit of an exasperated side to her, which shows when handling Charon, a bus driver with no idea how to use a map. However this situation only goes on to permeate Yuri's kindness when she later expresses wanting to properly teach her.

### Story
**Prior to Limbus Company***

Before becoming a Fixer, Yuri was affiliated with Lobotomy Corporation as a member of its Control Team.[1] She worked at Branch D-02, which she would later lead the Sinners through on their search for its Golden Bough. Lobotomy Corporation workers knew well that Abnormalities simply cannot die, and are simply reduced to a condensed ovate form when defeated, which eventually hatches once enough time has passed. While employed by L Corp., Yuri's job was to take these newly-created cores and put them back in their containment unit. However, at one point the L Corp. branch was locked down, and the building was set to come crashing down so that a breach of Abnormalities could not escape into the general City. Yuri found herself in the midst of this mass burial in the making with only three minutes until everything was shut down. With the immense pressure, danger, and knowledge that the doors were about to close on her, Yuri took the chance to escape, despite the colleagues begging her not to leave them behind. She was the only one out of her many coworkers to make it out and live on. From that day on, Yuri would live in masses of silent guilt, blaming herself and wondering if it was okay for her to survive alone. Following the incident, Yuri managed to secure a job as a Fixer, although only as a contract worker. Her job was specifically to deal with requests pertaining to the old L Corp. and help to make trips through it safer. She informs the Sinners that her contract may be extended if she manages good results on her trip with them.

**Canto I: The Outcast**

Yuri was initially introduced due to being hired by Faust to act as a guide for the Sinners during their first foray into the Lobotomy Corp. Branches. She introduced herself to the Sinners as a former member of the fallen Wing, only to later be baffled by the choice of Charon to drive without the guidance of a map. She was joined by Sinclair in an attempt to manage the driver, who would pay no heed to the two. Upon arriving closer to the Lobotomy Corp. Branch, the group was halted by members of the former G Corp., before meeting with Hopkins and Aya, who acted as accompanying Fixers.
In the midst of their journey, the group were interrupted by an unprompted attack by Abnormalities, as well as the G Corp. Head Manager. Beyond a point, toxicity levels within the building began to rise dramatically due to anti-Abnormality gas grenades, something which brings Yuri great distress due to her currently unprepared nature. Hopkins, however, is able to put on a gasmask he brought along, managing to use this as a moment to insult Yuri, before escaping with Enkephalin modules. Gregor gave Yuri the deceased Aya's gasmask, allowing her to survive the gas levels while the Sinners would simply revive from. She was comforted by Gregor as she malaises on her past, wondering if it was truly okay to have left behind her coworkers.
Continuing deeper into the branch, they would encounter Alex, one of the only surviving friends of Yuri, now driven insane due to her presence around the Doomsday Calendar Abnormality. The two coworkers would say their goodbyes to one another. As the Sinners would be thrust into the Smoke War through the Golden Bough's Resonance with Gregor, Yuri would firsthand experience the discomfort of the event as they continued deeper into the resonating Lobotomy Corp. Branch. The Sinners would begin to form a bond with Yuri, with Rodion jokingly raising the concept of the Fixer later being the LCB mascot. She would further be accepted into the group, before the group later encounters one of the Abnormalities stored in the branch, the Golden Apple.
As the Sinners combat the Abnormality, Yuri attempted to support the group, with Gregor joining her, though she would be absorbed by the Abnormality. The apple replicated Yuri, with Gregor being unable to strike her down due to the fake Yuri pleading for her life. The head was ultimately removed by Hermann, completing her progeny's job as she and N Corp. claim the Golden Bough within the branch. Gregor chose to position Yuri's gasmask on the front of Mephistopheles in memento, recalling his sister at the time.

---

## Zigong

### Appearance
Zigong is a woman with long black hair with several strands of red hair throughout, wrapped into a small bun atop her head secured by a gold hair ornament. She wears a dark hanfu that reach her ankles and dark armor on her torso and left bicep, the armpiece featuring a red band tied around it. Around her waist is a thick sash with a snakeskin patterning. Her robes split to reveal a white inside from the waist down, ending at her feet adorned in dark loafers.
She carries a gunbai with a patterning of flowers on the backside. The end of her gunbai appears to be charred.

### Personality
Zigong is a cryptic and cunning woman, choosing to respond to questions indirectly. Like her master, she values the price of information, speaking carefully and listening closely to others. She is highly perceptive, shown to be able to recognize the presence of a serpentine Heishou Pack member that her master was unaware of. Despite her intensive planning and wealth of knowledge, she recognizes her inability to account for everything in the formation of her plans, with enough humility to recognize how much more she has to learn. She frequently recites many of the teachings from her master when applicable. While Zigong is not seen fighting, Jia Qiu implies she is a very capable fighter, having planned on stalling the Thumb forces with her assisting him.[1] Nonetheless, she appears to prefer being away from the action, unlike Zilu.

### Story
**Intervallo V: Nocturnal Sweeping**

Accompanying her master, Zigong met the Sinners first as Shi Yihua was confronted over his attempted betrayal of his lord. Zigong recognized the presence of a Heishou Pack member with a serpentine appearance, yet was told to allow them to do as they like by Jia Qiu. Following the beheading of Shi Yihua by the mysterious Heishou Pack member, she reminded her lord of the process of using a stasis wrap to preserve both Yihua and Qingtao's heads. While her lord left without her, she chose to stay to shortly converse with Dante. During her brief discussion with the group, she recognized Jia Xichun and Hong Lu as insufficient to be rivals to her lord, meaning she has no concern with dispatching them. Despite this, she deflected on answering when Dante asked how this can be, following the attempted killing of the group at Shi Yihua's hands. Reminding the Sinners to 'remain within their borders', she left the area alongside Zilu.

**Canto VIII: The Surrendered Witnessing**

Following the first round of the Family Hierarch Evaluations, Zigong congratulated Hong Lu for passing, though scolded him for not heeding her prior words. Engaging in a short exchange of words, she called Outis' bluff when the opposing woman claimed Limbus Company's back-up would support the Sinners if confronted.
While Jia Qiu was accompanied by Zilu during the second round of the war, Zigong was not present alongside them. When her master forfeits the second round, and forewarned the Sinners of the growing turmoil and possibility of an oncoming war of the Wings, she sheepishly suggested a plan of hers that Jia Qiu chose to not abide by. Instead, he gave Hong Lu the option to participate in the ensuring of Jia Xichun's acquisition of the role of hierarch and the removal of the Xianren from power.
After the success of getting Jia Xichun out of the Tiekan Temple and to the Daguanyuan throne, Zigong accepted her failure as a retainer in her morbid plan, which involved gouging out Hong Lu's jade eye in order to enter Tiekan Temple. Kong Qiu's teasing makes her admit that she still has much to learn. Finally, she reminds Faust that discussing Kong Qiu's allegiance to the Pinky is not to be done lightly, if ever. Accompanying her master, she goes to see him off as he travels out of the District again, while she and Zilu are ordered to remain in Hongyuan to teach help Jia Xichun on what being the Hierarch of Hongyuan means.

**Intervallo VI: Spring Cultivation**

In the midst of a meeting of Hongyuan's associates and board of directors, Zigong enters to declare the importance of Jia Xichun learning how to assume her role, speaking down to Jia Yuanchun for leading the conversation, despite being an outsider. After a moment of discussion, the group is given the chance for a month of training Jia Xichun, after which she'll be tested on her capabilities.
Alongside Zilu, and per the instructions of Saude, Zigong assisted in forming the regimen used to train Jia Xichun and Sinclair. However, she did not participate in the training itself, having been saddled with the paperwork done for documenting all of Hongyuan, sending her temporarily into a delirious, insomniac state.
At the completion of the month-long training period, Jia Xichun took a trapped palanquin to what she assumed to be the site of her final test--in reality Jia Yuanchun aimed to have her covertly killed. Zigong quickly helped with recalibrating the plan upon learning this, sending the Sinners to save her.
After being saved, Jia Xichun's hearing was witnessed by the variety of involved factions, including Zigong.

### Trivia
Zigong's name stems from one of Chinese philosopher Kong Qiu's disciples, Duanmu Ci, who would go by Zigong (Mandarin: 子贡, Pinyin: Zǐgòng*) as his courtesy name.

---

## Zilu

### Appearance
Zilu is an imposing woman with dark hair and a bandaged face, wearing a wide-brimmed straw hat wrapped with cloth, two strands of which hang off the hat, ending in a bright yellow color. She wears a bulky gray and segmented scarf over a set of robes, a thick chain across her chest that holds a large greatsword sheathed in a canister on her back. Her arms are wrapped in the same cloth that covers her face, with her hands ending in sharp claws. Her multi-layered robes have a pattern of two yellow-eyed hares along the hem.
In Intervallo VI: Spring Cultivation, she is seen dressed more casually, with her face no longer bandaged. Blunt bangs cover her right eye. She wears dark robes with gray stripes over its sleeves, overtop a lighter gray hanfu folded over the left side of her chest. She has a set of cross-patterned dark straps visible beneath her robes. Her legs are visible, wearing thin leggings and tall-heeled shoes. The inner side of her robe is yellow. A small, white bunny pin sits on her left breast.

### Personality
Zilu is a quiet person, following orders closely without spending time on idle talk. She is highly professional, choosing to remind her companions of not speaking about important matters in front of enemies. She remains highly loyal to Jia Qiu, returning to his side immediately upon his arrival, unfazed by the death of Shi Yihua. Her loyalty extends so far as to willingly sacrifice herself for those her master trusts, even if for others she has no connection to.
Intervallo VI: Spring Cultivation reveals a more casual side of Zilu, where she speaks casually to others. She is shown to be sensitive, feeling guilt over the fact of having to tell Sinclair he will not be participating after the Sinner's excitement for creating a teaching regimen. She is also shown to be very sarcastic, asking the Sinners to consider how Meursault's lesson plan (being idle for a week without any orders) makes for a good Hierarch, and calling Zigong a slacker under her breath for leaving the entire 30-day lesson plans to Zilu and Saude.

### Story
**Intervallo V: Nocturnal Sweeping**

As the Family Hierarch Evaluation drew near, Jia Qiu, Zilu's master, allowed Shi Yihua to temporarily use Zilu and the other Heishou Pack Mao Branch members. Shi Yihua schemed to allow his family a greater standing among families, leading him to hiring several factions and people to assist him in securing a lead in the examinations.
As a part of Shi Yihua's plan, once the Sinners arrived in H Corp., they were led to Qingtao's trapped kezhan, and once they went to rest for the night, the Heishou Pack's Mao Branch began attacking the Sinners, killing several before being fended off. As they moved back to the central lounge, Shi Yihua and Zilu revealed themselves, beginning combat against the group. This fight would be cut short however, as Ricardo, a Big Brother of the Middle, appeared alongside a handful of Little Brothers who attacked those present. At the summit of the fight, Shi Yihua and Zilu fled to allow the Sweepers to deal with their enemies.
Having expected the Sweepers to kill Sinners and the Middle, the two prepared a final assault on the Sinners, though they did not get the chance to begin the attack as Jia Qiu and Zigong arrived. He exposed Shi Yihua's plot to give his family greater influence, which resulted in Shi Yihua begging his life. Shi Yihua started to share secrets of the Shi family, but before he could share anything of importance, a Si Branch Heishou Pack member appeared and decapitated him. Jia Qiu told Zilu that there was no need to pursue the serpent and to return to him once she had finished the job, then left carrying the decapitated heads of Qingtao and Shi Yihua. Zigong reasoned that he would not have left the Sinners and Jia Xichun alive if he had wanted them dead, so she and Zilu soon left and returned to their master.

**Canto VIII: The Surrendered Witnessing**

Following the first round of the Family Hierarch Evaluations, Zilu accompanied her lord as he briefly exchanged words with Hong Lu.
During the second round of the war, Zilu battled her master's opponents alongside him. During battle against Hong Lu, she repeatedly joined combat at her master's word, while he attempted to parlay a true answer of what Hongyuan needs from his younger opponent.
Zilu was left in charge of forwarding information to Jia Qiu pertaining to external forces looking to cause a war of the Wings via abusing the power vacuum left prior to Jia Xichun's ascension to hierarch. Jia Qiu, looking to ensure Xichun's rise and the fall of the Xianren, requested the alliance alongside Hong Lu, to which he accepts. In return, he sends Zilu to meet up with the Sinners outside the Tiekan Temple, though she would not accompany them on the path to it.
Outside the temple, the Sinners encountered Lei Heng, a Capo IIII of the Thumb, and an incognito member of the Pinky. Zilu joins them via a makeshift passageway, having visibly battled other forces on her way there. In exchange for Wei's ensured safety, Lei Heng looks to land a single blow on Zilu, who he exposes as another member of the Pinky; Meizhelen the Tianjiu Star, the Unrestrained. Hong Lu, recognizing this would help Xichun be happy again, accepted Zilu's offer to do this. Using Shin to guard herself, Lei Heng viciously wounded her, leaving her unable to battle. A man of his word however, he kicked Wei to them. Zilu attempted to regain her strength until her master arrived, who battled in their stead as they continued through the temple. Despite her grievous injury, Zilu survived the encounter.
Days later, as the role of H Corp. Hierarch was secured by Xichun, accompanied her master to see him off as he travels out of the District again, while she and Zigong are ordered to remain in Hongyuan to teach help Jia Xichun on what being the Hierarch of Hongyuan means. While the group planned to continue on their path as members of the Pinky, Zigong reminded the faction of not discussing the faction's connection to the Finger lightly.

**Intervallo VI: Spring Cultivation**

Alongside Zigong, and per the instructions of Saude, Zilu assisted in forming the regimen used to train Jia Xichun and Sinclair. Given the task of primary instructor, she was tasked with the formation of each Sinners' specialty applying to a lecture. While this took her several attempts for several of the Sinners, scrapping several of the works in progress that would not suffice, she ultimately formed the most pertinent of lessons among the twelve instructors.
Forming a training set into Zhi, Yong, and Ren, Zilu instructed Jia Xichun on what she will be expected to have taken from each of the lessons she would be in over the course of the month. During this period, she spectated the training of the duo.
On one day of training, while spectating, Zilu was suddenly interested in the teachings of the Night Drifter, who she recognized as a former member of the Ten Blades of the East, though he brushed this off.
After being saved from a botched assassination attempt, Jia Xichun's hearing was witnessed by the variety of involved factions, including Zilu.

### Trivia
Zilu's name stems from one of Chinese philosopher Kong Qiu's disciples, Zhong You, who would go by Zilu (Mandarin: 子路, Pinyin: Zǐlù) as his courtesy name.
Zilu's title as the Tianjiu Star references Mu Hong from Water Margin*, who corresponds to the Tianjiu Star (天究星), the "Investigative Star", who is ranked 24th among the outlaws.

---
